`Introduction`
--------------

**_é€‚ç”¨äºæ‰€æœ‰äººçš„JavaScript_**æ˜¯é¢å‘åˆå­¦è€…å’Œé«˜çº§JavaScriptå¼€å‘äººå‘˜çš„æŒ‡å—ã€‚æ¬¢è¿ä½¿ç”¨JavaScriptã€‚**_æ­å–œ_**æ‚¨å†³å®šå­¦ä¹ JavaScriptï¼Œå³æµè§ˆå™¨çš„è¯­è¨€ã€‚

åœ¨æœ¬åˆ†æ­¥æ•™ç¨‹ä¸­ï¼Œæ‚¨å°†å­¦ä¹ JavaScriptï¼Œè¿™æ˜¯äººç±»å†å²ä¸Šæœ€æµè¡Œçš„ç¼–ç¨‹è¯­è¨€ã€‚æ‚¨ä½¿ç”¨JavaScript**_å‘ç½‘ç«™æ·»åŠ äº¤äº’æ€§ï¼Œå¼€å‘ç§»åŠ¨åº”ç”¨ç¨‹åºï¼Œæ¡Œé¢åº”ç”¨ç¨‹åºï¼Œæ¸¸æˆ_**ï¼Œå¦‚ä»ŠJavaScriptå¯ç”¨äº**_æœºå™¨å­¦ä¹ _**å’Œ**_AI_**ã€‚ è¿‘å¹´æ¥ï¼Œ**_JavaScriptï¼ˆJSï¼‰_**è¶Šæ¥è¶Šæµè¡Œï¼Œå¹¶ä¸”å·²ç»è¿ç»­å››å¹´æˆä¸ºé¢†å…ˆçš„ç¼–ç¨‹è¯­è¨€ï¼Œå¹¶ä¸”æ˜¯Githubä¸Šä½¿ç”¨æœ€å¤šçš„ç¼–ç¨‹è¯­è¨€ã€‚

é¦–å…ˆï¼Œè®©æˆ‘ä»¬å®‰è£…æ–‡æœ¬æˆ–ä»£ç ç¼–è¾‘å™¨ã€‚å®‰è£…ä»£ç ç¼–è¾‘å™¨ï¼Œå¯ä»¥æ˜¯[vscode](https://code.visualstudio.com/)ï¼Œ[atom](https://atom.io/)ï¼Œ[bracket](http://brackets.io/)ï¼Œ[notepad ++](https://notepad-plus-plus.org/)æˆ–å…¶ä»–ã€‚æˆ‘æ¨èvscodeã€‚å¦‚æœè¿˜æ²¡æœ‰ï¼Œè¯·å®‰è£…[Chrome](https://www.google.com/chrome/)æˆ–[Firefox](https://www.mozilla.org/en-US/firefox/new/?v=b)ã€‚

å¦‚æœéœ€è¦å¸®åŠ©ï¼Œå¯ä»¥åŠ å…¥[ç”µæŠ¥](https://t.me/JavaScriptforEveryone)é¢‘é“ã€‚

### `Install Node.js`

æ‚¨ç°åœ¨å¯èƒ½ä¸éœ€è¦å®ƒï¼Œä½†ä»¥åå¯èƒ½éœ€è¦å®ƒã€‚å®‰è£…[çš„node.js](https://nodejs.org/en/)ã€‚

](https://github.com/Asabeneh/JavaScript-for-Everyone/blob/master/images/download_node.png)

ä¸‹è½½ååŒå‡»å®‰è£…

[![](https://github.com/Asabeneh/JavaScript-for-Everyone/raw/master/images/install_node.png)
](https://github.com/Asabeneh/JavaScript-for-Everyone/blob/master/images/install_node.png)

æˆ‘ä»¬å¯ä»¥é€šè¿‡æ‰“å¼€è®¾å¤‡ç»ˆç«¯æˆ–å‘½ä»¤æç¤ºç¬¦æ¥æ£€æŸ¥æ˜¯å¦åœ¨æœ¬åœ°è®¡ç®—æœºä¸­å®‰è£…äº†èŠ‚ç‚¹ã€‚

```shell

v12.14.0
```

##### `Syntax`

JavaScriptæ˜¯ä¸€ç§ç¼–ç¨‹è¯­è¨€ã€‚ç»“æœï¼Œå®ƒå…·æœ‰ä¸å…¶ä»–ç¼–ç¨‹è¯­è¨€ä¸€æ ·çš„è¯­æ³•ã€‚å¦‚æœæˆ‘ä»¬æ²¡æœ‰ç¼–å†™JavaScriptå¯ä»¥ç†è§£çš„è¯­æ³•ï¼Œå®ƒå°†å¼•å‘ä¸åŒç±»å‹çš„é”™è¯¯ã€‚ç¨åæˆ‘ä»¬å°†æ¢è®¨å„ç§JavaScripté”™è¯¯ã€‚ç°åœ¨ï¼Œè®©æˆ‘ä»¬çœ‹çœ‹è¯­æ³•é”™è¯¯ã€‚

[![](https://github.com/Asabeneh/JavaScript-for-Everyone/raw/master/images/raising_syntax_error.png)
](https://github.com/Asabeneh/JavaScript-for-Everyone/blob/master/images/raising_syntax_error.png)

æˆ‘æ•…æ„çŠ¯äº†ä¸€ä¸ªé”™è¯¯ã€‚ç»“æœï¼Œæ§åˆ¶å°å¼•å‘è¯­æ³•é”™è¯¯ã€‚å®é™…ä¸Šï¼Œè¯­æ³•éå¸¸æœ‰ç”¨ã€‚å®ƒå‘ŠçŸ¥æˆ‘ä»¬çŠ¯äº†å“ªç§ç±»å‹çš„é”™è¯¯ã€‚é€šè¿‡é˜…è¯»é”™è¯¯åé¦ˆæŒ‡å—ï¼Œæˆ‘ä»¬å¯ä»¥æ›´æ­£è¯­æ³•å¹¶è§£å†³é—®é¢˜ã€‚ä»ç¨‹åºä¸­è¯†åˆ«å’Œæ¶ˆé™¤é”™è¯¯çš„è¿‡ç¨‹ç§°ä¸ºè°ƒè¯•ã€‚è®©æˆ‘ä»¬ä¿®å¤é”™è¯¯ï¼š

```js
console.log("Hello, World!")
console.log('Hello, World!')
```

åˆ°ç›®å‰ä¸ºæ­¢ï¼Œæˆ‘ä»¬å·²ç»çœ‹åˆ°äº†å¦‚ä½•ä½¿ç”¨_console.logï¼ˆï¼‰_æ˜¾ç¤ºæ–‡æœ¬ã€‚å¦‚æœæˆ‘ä»¬ä½¿ç”¨_console.logï¼ˆï¼‰_æ‰“å°æ–‡æœ¬æˆ–å­—ç¬¦ä¸²ï¼Œåˆ™æ–‡æœ¬å¿…é¡»åœ¨å•å¼•å·ï¼ŒåŒå¼•å·æˆ–åå¼•å·ä¸‹ã€‚ **ä¾‹ï¼š**

#### `Arithmetics`

ç°åœ¨ï¼Œè®©æˆ‘ä»¬ç»ƒä¹ æ›´å¤šä½¿ç”¨google chromeæ§åˆ¶å°ä¸Šçš„_console.logï¼ˆï¼‰_ç¼–å†™æ•°å­—æ•°æ®ç±»å‹çš„JavaScriptä»£ç ã€‚é™¤äº†æ–‡æœ¬ä¹‹å¤–ï¼Œæˆ‘ä»¬è¿˜å¯ä»¥ä½¿ç”¨JavaScriptè¿›è¡Œæ•°å­¦è®¡ç®—ã€‚è®©æˆ‘ä»¬è¿›è¡Œä»¥ä¸‹ç®€å•è®¡ç®—ã€‚

[![](https://github.com/Asabeneh/JavaScript-for-Everyone/raw/master/images/arithmetic.png)
](https://github.com/Asabeneh/JavaScript-for-Everyone/blob/master/images/arithmetic.png)

```js
console.log(2 + 3)   // Addition
console.log(3 - 2)   // Subtraction
console.log(2 * 3)   // Multiplication  
console.log(3 / 2)   // Division
console.log(3 % 2)   // Modulus - finding remainder
console.log(3 ** 2)  // Exponential
```

å¯ä»¥é€šè¿‡ä»¥ä¸‹ä¸‰ç§æ–¹å¼å°†JavaScriptæ·»åŠ åˆ°ç½‘é¡µä¸­ï¼š

*   **_å†…è”è„šæœ¬_**

ä»¥ä¸‹å„èŠ‚æ˜¾ç¤ºäº†å°†JavaScriptä»£ç æ·»åŠ åˆ°ç½‘é¡µçš„ä¸åŒæ–¹æ³•ã€‚

#### `Inline Script`

åœ¨æ‚¨çš„æ¡Œé¢æˆ–ä»»ä½•ä½ç½®åˆ›å»ºä¸€ä¸ªæ–‡ä»¶å¤¹ï¼Œå¹¶åœ¨è¯¥æ–‡ä»¶å¤¹ä¸­åˆ›å»ºä¸€ä¸ª**_index.html_**æ–‡ä»¶ã€‚ç„¶åç²˜è´´ä»¥ä¸‹ä»£ç ï¼Œå¹¶åœ¨[Chrome](https://www.google.com/chrome/)æˆ–[Firefox](https://www.mozilla.org/en-US/firefox/new/?v=b)æµè§ˆå™¨ä¸­æ‰“å¼€å®ƒã€‚

```html
<!DOCTYPE html>
  <html>
    <head>
      <title>JavaScript for Everyone</title>
    </head>
    <body>
      <button onclick="alert('Welcome to JavaScript!');">Click Me</button>
    </body>
  </html>
```

#### `Internal script`

å†…éƒ¨è„šæœ¬å¯ä»¥å†™åœ¨_å¤´éƒ¨_æˆ–_æ­£æ–‡ä¸­ï¼Œ_ä½†æœ€å¥½å°†å…¶æ”¾åœ¨htmlæ–‡æ¡£çš„æ­£æ–‡ä¸­ã€‚

*   å†…éƒ¨è„šæœ¬åœ¨å¤´

```html
<!DOCTYPE html>
  <html>
    <head>
      <title>JavaScript for Everyone</title>
      <script>
        console.log("Welcome to JavaScript for Everyone");
      </script>
    </head>
    <body>
  
    </body>
  </html>
```

*   èº«ä½“å†…éƒ¨çš„å‰§æœ¬

```html
<!DOCTYPE html>
  <html>
    <head>
      <title>JavaScript for Everyone</title>
    </head>
    <body>
      <script>
        console.log("Welcome to JavaScript for Everyone");
      </script>
    </body>
  </html>
```

#### `External script`

å¤–éƒ¨è„šæœ¬é“¾æ¥å¯ä»¥ä½äºå¤´éƒ¨æˆ–èº«ä½“ä¸Šï¼Œä½†æœ€å¥½å°†å…¶æ”¾åœ¨èº«ä½“ä¸­ã€‚

*   å¤–éƒ¨è„šæœ¬åœ¨å¤´

```html

  <html>
    <head>
      <title>JavaScript for Everyone</title>
      <script src="introduction.js"></script>
    </head>
    <body>
    </body>
    </html
```

*   èº«ä½“å¤–éƒ¨è„šæœ¬

```html
<!DOCTYPE html>
  <html>
    <head>
      <title>JavaScript for Everyone</title>
    </head>
    <body>
      //it could be in the header or in the body
      // Here is the recommended place to put the script
      <script src="introduction.js"></script>
    </body>
    </html
```

### `Exercises:Setting Up your machine`

`Variables`
-----------

å˜é‡æ˜¯æ•°æ®çš„_å®¹å™¨_ã€‚å˜é‡_å°†_æ•°æ®_å­˜å‚¨_åœ¨å†…å­˜ä½ç½®ã€‚å£°æ˜å˜é‡æ—¶ï¼Œå°†ä¿ç•™å­˜å‚¨ä½ç½®ï¼Œå¹¶å°†å…¶åˆ†é…ç»™å€¼æ—¶ï¼Œå°†å¡«å……å­˜å‚¨ç©ºé—´ã€‚è¦å£°æ˜å˜é‡ï¼Œæˆ‘ä»¬ä½¿ç”¨_var_ï¼Œ_let_æˆ–_const_å…³é”®å­—ã€‚å¯¹äºåœ¨ä¸åŒæ—¶é—´æ›´æ”¹çš„å˜é‡ï¼Œæˆ‘ä»¬ä½¿ç”¨_letï¼Œ_ä½†å¦‚æœæ•°æ®å®Œå…¨ä¸å˜ï¼Œåˆ™ä½¿ç”¨_const_ã€‚ä¾‹å¦‚PIï¼Œå›½å®¶åç§°ï¼Œé‡åŠ›ã€‚

*   JavaScriptå˜é‡åç§°ä¸åº”ä»¥æ•°å­—å¼€å¤´
*   JavaScriptå˜é‡åç§°ä¸å…è®¸ä½¿ç”¨ç‰¹æ®Šå­—ç¬¦ï¼Œä½†ç¾å…ƒç¬¦å·å’Œä¸‹åˆ’çº¿é™¤å¤–ã€‚
*   JavaScriptå˜é‡åç§°éµå¾ªcamelCaseçº¦å®šã€‚
*   JavaScriptå˜é‡åç§°çš„å•è¯ä¹‹é—´ä¸åº”æœ‰ç©ºæ ¼ã€‚ä»¥ä¸‹æ˜¯JavaScriptå˜é‡çš„æœ‰æ•ˆç¤ºä¾‹ã€‚

JavaScriptä¸­çš„æœ‰æ•ˆå˜é‡ï¼š

```js
    firstName
    lastName
    country
    city
    capitalCity
    age
    isMarried

    first_name
    last_name
    is_married
    capital_city

    num1
    num_1
    _num_1
    $num1
    year2019
    year_2019
```

Camel caseï¼ˆcamelCaseï¼‰æˆ–ç¬¬ä¸€ç§å£°æ˜æ–¹å¼æ˜¯JavaScriptä¸­çš„å¸¸è§„æ–¹æ³•ã€‚åœ¨æ­¤ææ–™ä¸­ï¼Œå°†ä½¿ç”¨camelCaseå˜é‡ã€‚

æ— æ•ˆçš„å˜é‡ï¼š

å£°æ˜å˜é‡

```js
// Declaring different variables of different data types

let firstName = 'Asabeneh'; // first name of a person
let lastName = 'Yetayeh';   // last name of a person
let country = 'Finland';    // country
let city = 'Helsinki';      // capital city
let age = 100;              // age in years
let isMarried = true;
console.log(firstName, lastName, country, city, age, isMarried); // Asabeneh, Yetayeh, Finland, Helsinki, 100, True

// Declaring variables with number values

const gravity = 9.81;                    // earth gravity  in m/s2
const boilingPoint = 100;                // water boiling point, temperature in oC
const PI = 3.14;                         // geometrical constant
console.log(gravity, boilingPoint, PI);  // 9.81, 100, 3.14

// Variables can also be declaring in one line separated by comma

let name = 'Asabeneh', //name of a person
  job = 'teacher',
  live = 'Finland';
console.log(name, job, live);
```

### `Exercise - 1 : Variables`

1.  åœ¨ä¸åˆ†é…å€¼çš„æƒ…å†µä¸‹å£°æ˜å››ä¸ªå˜é‡
    
2.  å£°æ˜å››ä¸ªå˜é‡å¹¶èµ‹å€¼
    
3.  å£°æ˜å˜é‡ä»¥å¤šè¡Œå­˜å‚¨æ‚¨çš„åå­—ï¼Œå§“æ°ï¼Œå©šå§»çŠ¶å†µï¼Œå›½å®¶å’Œå¹´é¾„
    
4.  å£°æ˜å˜é‡ä»¥åœ¨ä¸€è¡Œä¸­å­˜å‚¨æ‚¨çš„åå­—ï¼Œå§“æ°ï¼Œå©šå§»çŠ¶å†µï¼Œå›½å®¶å’Œå¹´é¾„
    
5.  å£°æ˜ä¸¤ä¸ªå˜é‡_myAge_å’Œ_yourAge_å¹¶ä¸ºå…¶åˆ†é…åˆå§‹å€¼ï¼Œç„¶åç™»å½•åˆ°æµè§ˆå™¨æ§åˆ¶å°ã€‚è¾“å‡ºï¼š
    
    ```shell
    I am 25 years old.
    You are 30 years old.
    ```
    

`Comments`
----------

JavaScriptä¸­çš„æ³¨é‡Šä¸å…¶ä»–ç¼–ç¨‹è¯­è¨€ç±»ä¼¼ã€‚æ³¨é‡Šå¯ä»¥å¸®åŠ©æé«˜ä»£ç çš„å¯è¯»æ€§ã€‚æœ‰ä¸¤ç§è¯„è®ºæ–¹å¼ï¼š

*   _å•è¡Œæ³¨é‡Š_
*   _å¤šè¡Œè¯„è®º_

```js
// let firstName = 'Asabeneh'; single line comment
// let lastName = 'Yetayeh'; single line comment
```

å¤šè¡Œè¯„è®ºï¼š

```js

    let location = 'Helsinki';
    let age = 100;
    let isMarried = true;
    This is a Multiple line comment
    */
```

### `Exercise: Comments`

1.  å†™ä¸€è¡Œæ³¨é‡Šï¼Œ_æ³¨é‡Šå¯ä»¥ä½¿ä»£ç å¯è¯»_
2.  ç¼–å†™å¤šè¡Œæ³¨é‡Šï¼Œå…¶ä¸­_æ³¨é‡Šå¯ä»¥ä½¿ä»£ç æ˜“è¯»ï¼Œæ˜“ç”¨_ _ä¸”ä¿¡æ¯ä¸°å¯Œ_

`Data types`
------------

åœ¨ä¸Šä¸€èŠ‚ä¸­ï¼Œæˆ‘ä»¬æåˆ°äº†ä¸€äº›æœ‰å…³æ•°æ®ç±»å‹çš„å†…å®¹ã€‚æ•°æ®æˆ–å€¼å…·æœ‰æ•°æ®ç±»å‹ã€‚æ•°æ®ç±»å‹æè¿°æ•°æ®çš„ç‰¹å¾ã€‚æ•°æ®ç±»å‹å¯ä»¥åˆ†ä¸ºä¸¤ç§

1.  åŸå§‹æ•°æ®ç±»å‹
2.  éåŸå§‹æ•°æ®ç±»å‹ï¼ˆå¯¹è±¡å¼•ç”¨ï¼‰

### `Primitive Data Types`

JavaScriptä¸­çš„åŸå§‹æ•°æ®ç±»å‹åŒ…æ‹¬ï¼š

1.  æ•°å­—-æ•´æ•°ï¼Œæµ®ç‚¹æ•°
2.  å­—ç¬¦ä¸²-å•å¼•å·æˆ–åŒå¼•å·ä¸‹çš„ä»»ä½•æ•°æ®
3.  å¸ƒå°”å€¼-çœŸæˆ–å‡å€¼
4.  ç©º-ç©ºå€¼æˆ–æ— å€¼
5.  æœªå®šä¹‰-æ²¡æœ‰å€¼çš„å£°æ˜å˜é‡

JavaScriptä¸­çš„éåŸå§‹æ•°æ®ç±»å‹åŒ…æ‹¬ï¼š

1.  å¯¹è±¡
2.  èŒèƒ½
3.  æ•°ç»„

ç°åœ¨ï¼Œè®©æˆ‘ä»¬æ¥çœ‹ä¸€ä¸‹åŸå§‹å’ŒéåŸå§‹æ•°æ®ç±»å‹çš„ç¡®åˆ‡å«ä¹‰ã€‚ _åŸºæœ¬_æ•°æ®ç±»å‹æ˜¯ä¸å¯å˜ï¼ˆä¸å¯ä¿®æ”¹ï¼‰æ•°æ®ç±»å‹ã€‚åˆ›å»ºåŸå§‹æ•°æ®ç±»å‹åï¼Œæˆ‘ä»¬å°†æ— æ³•å¯¹å…¶è¿›è¡Œä¿®æ”¹ã€‚ **ä¾‹ï¼š** 

å¦‚æœæˆ‘ä»¬å°è¯•ä¿®æ”¹å­˜å‚¨åœ¨å˜é‡_wordä¸­_çš„å­—ç¬¦ä¸²ï¼ŒJavaScriptå°†å¼•å‘é”™è¯¯ã€‚å•å¼•å·ï¼ŒåŒå¼•å·æˆ–åå¼•å·ä¸‹çš„ä»»ä½•æ•°æ®ç±»å‹éƒ½æ˜¯å­—ç¬¦ä¸²æ•°æ®ç±»å‹ã€‚

æ­¤è¡¨è¾¾å¼ä¸ä¼šæ›´æ”¹å­˜å‚¨åœ¨å˜é‡_wordä¸­_çš„å­—ç¬¦ä¸²ã€‚å› æ­¤ï¼Œæˆ‘ä»¬å¯ä»¥è¯´å­—ç¬¦ä¸²ä¸å¯ä¿®æ”¹æˆ–ä¸å¯å˜ã€‚é€šè¿‡å…¶å€¼æ¯”è¾ƒåŸå§‹æ•°æ®ç±»å‹ã€‚è®©æˆ‘ä»¬æ¯”è¾ƒä¸åŒçš„æ•°æ®å€¼ã€‚è¯·å‚é˜…ä»¥ä¸‹ç¤ºä¾‹ï¼š

```js
let numOne = 3
let numTwo = 3

console.log(numOne == numTwo)      // true

let js = 'JavaScript'
let py = 'Python'

console.log(js == py)             //false 

let lightOn = true
let lightOff = false

console.log(lightOn == lightOff) // false
```

### `Non-Primitive Data Types`

_éåŸå§‹_æ•°æ®ç±»å‹æ˜¯å¯ä¿®æ”¹æˆ–å¯å˜çš„ã€‚åˆ›å»ºéåŸå§‹æ•°æ®ç±»å‹åï¼Œæˆ‘ä»¬å¯ä»¥ä¿®æ”¹å…¶å€¼ã€‚è®©æˆ‘ä»¬é€šè¿‡åˆ›å»ºä¸€ä¸ªæ•°ç»„æ¥çœ‹çœ‹ã€‚æ•°ç»„æ˜¯æ–¹æ‹¬å·ä¸­çš„æ•°æ®å€¼åˆ—è¡¨ã€‚æ•°ç»„å¯ä»¥åŒ…å«ç›¸åŒæˆ–ä¸åŒçš„æ•°æ®ç±»å‹ã€‚æ•°ç»„å€¼ç”±å…¶ç´¢å¼•å¼•ç”¨ã€‚åœ¨JavaScriptä¸­ï¼Œæ•°ç»„ç´¢å¼•ä»é›¶å¼€å§‹ã€‚å³ï¼Œæ•°ç»„çš„ç¬¬ä¸€ä¸ªå…ƒç´ ä½äºç´¢å¼•é›¶ï¼Œç¬¬äºŒä¸ªå…ƒç´ ä½äºç´¢å¼•ä¸€ï¼Œç¬¬ä¸‰ä¸ªå…ƒç´ ä½äºç´¢å¼•äºŒï¼Œä¾æ­¤ç±»æ¨ã€‚

```js
let nums = [1, 2, 3]
nums[0] = 10

console.log(nums)  // [10, 2, 3]
```

å¦‚æ‚¨æ‰€è§ï¼Œä¸€ä¸ªéåŸå§‹æ•°æ®ç±»å‹æ˜¯å¯å˜çš„æ•°ç»„ã€‚éåŸå§‹æ•°æ®ç±»å‹æ— æ³•æŒ‰å€¼è¿›è¡Œæ¯”è¾ƒã€‚å³ä½¿ä¸¤ä¸ªéåŸå§‹æ•°æ®ç±»å‹å…·æœ‰ç›¸åŒçš„å±æ€§å’Œå€¼ï¼Œå®ƒä»¬ä¹Ÿä¸æ˜¯ä¸¥æ ¼ç›¸ç­‰çš„ã€‚

```js
let nums = [1, 2, 3]
let numbers = [1, 2, 3]

console.log(nums == numbers)  // false

let userOne = {
name:'Asabeneh',
role:'teaching',
country:'Finland'
}

let userTwo = {
name:'Asabeneh',
role:'teaching',
country:'Finland'
}

console.log(userOne == userTwo) // false
```

æ ¹æ®ç»éªŒï¼Œæˆ‘ä»¬ä¸æ¯”è¾ƒéåŸå§‹æ•°æ®ç±»å‹ã€‚ä¸è¦æ¯”è¾ƒæ•°ç»„ï¼Œå‡½æ•°æˆ–å¯¹è±¡ã€‚éåŸå§‹å€¼ç§°ä¸ºå¼•ç”¨ç±»å‹ï¼Œå› ä¸ºå®ƒä»¬æ˜¯é€šè¿‡å¼•ç”¨è€Œä¸æ˜¯å€¼è¿›è¡Œæ¯”è¾ƒçš„ã€‚å¦‚æœä¸¤ä¸ªå¯¹è±¡å¼•ç”¨ç›¸åŒçš„åŸºç¡€å¯¹è±¡ï¼Œåˆ™å®ƒä»¬ä¸¥æ ¼ç›¸ç­‰ã€‚

```js
let nums = [1, 2, 3]
let numbers = nums

console.log(nums == numbers)  // true

let userOne = {
name:'Asabeneh',
role:'teaching',
country:'Finland'
}

let userTwo = userOne

console.log(userOne == userTwo)  // true
```

å¦‚æœæ‚¨å¾ˆéš¾ç†è§£åŸå§‹æ•°æ®ç±»å‹å’ŒéåŸå§‹æ•°æ®ç±»å‹ä¹‹é—´çš„åŒºåˆ«ï¼Œé‚£ä¹ˆæ‚¨ä¸æ˜¯å”¯ä¸€çš„äººã€‚å†·é™ä¸‹æ¥ï¼Œç„¶åè½¬åˆ°ä¸‹ä¸€éƒ¨åˆ†ï¼Œå°è¯•åœ¨ä¸€æ®µæ—¶é—´åå†å›æ¥ã€‚ç°åœ¨è®©æˆ‘ä»¬ä»æ•°å­—ç±»å‹å¼€å§‹æ•°æ®ç±»å‹ã€‚

`Numbers`
---------

æ•°å­—æ˜¯å¯ä»¥æ‰§è¡Œæ‰€æœ‰ç®—æœ¯è¿ç®—çš„æ•´æ•°å’Œåè¿›åˆ¶å€¼ã€‚è®©æˆ‘ä»¬æ¥çœ‹ä¸€äº›æ•°å­—ç¤ºä¾‹ã€‚

### `Declaring number data types`

```js
let age = 35
const gravity = 9.81  //we use const for non-changing values, gravitational constant in  m/s2
let mass = 72         // mass in Kilogram
const PI = 3.14       // pi a geometrical constant

//More Examples
const boilingPoint = 100 // temperature in oC, boiling point of water which is a constant
const bodyTemp = 37      // oC average human body temperature, which is a constant

console.log(age, gravity, mass, PI, boilingPoint, bodyTemp)
```

### `Math Object`

åœ¨JavaScriptä¸­ï¼Œæ•°å­¦å¯¹è±¡æä¾›äº†è®¸å¤šå¤„ç†æ•°å­—çš„æ–¹æ³•ã€‚

```js
const PI = Math.PI

console.log(PI)                           // 3.141592653589793

// Rounding to the closest number
// if above .5 up if less 0.5 down rounding

console.log(Math.round(PI))               // 3 to round values to the nearest number

console.log(Math.round(9.81))             // 10

console.log(Math.floor(PI))               // 3 rounding down

console.log(Math.ceil(PI))                // 4 rounding up

console.log(Math.min(-5, 3, 20, 4,5, 10)) // -5, returns the minimum value

console.log(Math.max(-5, 3, 20, 4,5, 10)) // 20, returns the maximum value

const randNum = Math.random() // creates random number between 0 to 0.999999
console.log(randNum)

// Let us  create random number between 0 to 10

const num = Math.floor(Math.random () * 11) // creates random number between 0 and 10
console.log(num)

//Absolute value
console.log(Math.abs(-10))      //10

//Square root
console.log(Math.sqrt(100))     // 10

console.log(Math.sqrt(2))      //1.4142135623730951

// Power
console.log(Math.pow(3, 2)) // 9

console.log(Math.E) // 2.718

// Logarithm
//Returns the natural logarithm of base E of x, Math.log(x)
console.log(Math.log(2))    // 0.6931471805599453
console.log(Math.log(10))   // 2.302585092994046

// Trigonometry
Math.sin(0)
Math.sin(60)

Math.cos(0)
Math.cos(60)
```

#### `Random number generator`

JavaScript Mathå¯¹è±¡å…·æœ‰ä¸€ä¸ªrandomï¼ˆï¼‰æ–¹æ³•ç¼–å·ç”Ÿæˆå™¨ï¼Œè¯¥ç”Ÿæˆå™¨ç”Ÿæˆä»0åˆ°0.999999999çš„æ•°å­—ã€‚

```js
let randomNum = Math.random() // generates 0 to 0.999
```

ç°åœ¨ï¼Œè®©æˆ‘ä»¬çœ‹çœ‹å¦‚ä½•ä½¿ç”¨randomï¼ˆï¼‰æ–¹æ³•ç”Ÿæˆä»‹äº0å’Œ10ä¹‹é—´ï¼ˆå«0å’Œ10ï¼‰çš„éšæœºæ•°ã€‚

```js
let randomNum = Math.random()         // generates 0 to 0.999
let numBtnZeroAndTen = randomNum * 11

console.log(numBtnZeroAndTen)         // this gives: min 0 and max 10.99

let randomNumRoundToFloor = Math.floor(numBtnZeroAndTen)
console.log(randomNumRoundToFloor)    // this gives between 0 and 10
```

`Strings`
---------

å­—ç¬¦ä¸²æ˜¯æ–‡æœ¬ï¼Œç”¨**_å•_**å¼•å·æˆ–**_åŒ_**å¼•å·å¼•èµ·æ¥ã€‚è¦å£°æ˜ä¸€ä¸ªå­—ç¬¦ä¸²ï¼Œæˆ‘ä»¬éœ€è¦ä¸€ä¸ªå˜é‡åï¼Œèµ‹å€¼è¿ç®—ç¬¦ï¼Œå•å¼•å·ï¼ŒåŒå¼•å·æˆ–åå¼•å·ä¸‹çš„å€¼ã€‚æˆ‘ä»¬æ¥çœ‹ä¸€äº›å­—ç¬¦ä¸²ç¤ºä¾‹ï¼š

```js
let space = ' '           // an empty space string
let firstName = 'Asabeneh'
let lastName = 'Yetayeh'
let country = 'Finland'
let city = 'Helsinki'
let language = 'JavaScript'
let job = 'teacher'
```

### `String Concatenation`

å°†ä¸¤ä¸ªæˆ–å¤šä¸ªå­—ç¬¦ä¸²è¿æ¥åœ¨ä¸€èµ·ç§°ä¸ºä¸²è”ã€‚

```js
// Declaring different variables of different data types
let space = ' '
let firstName = 'Asabeneh'
let lastName = 'Yetayeh'
let country = 'Finland'
let city = 'Helsinki'
let language = 'JavaScript'
let job = 'teacher'
```

```js
let fullName = firstName + space + lastName; // concatenation, merging two string together.
console.log(fullName);
```

æˆ‘ä»¬å¯ä»¥ç”¨ä¸åŒçš„æ–¹å¼è¿æ¥å­—ç¬¦ä¸²ã€‚

#### `Concatenating using addition operator`

ä½¿ç”¨åŠ æ³•è¿ç®—ç¬¦è¿›è¡Œè¿æ¥æ˜¯ä¸€ç§æ—§æ–¹æ³•ã€‚è¿™ç§è¿æ¥æ–¹å¼æ—¢ç¹çåˆå®¹æ˜“å‡ºé”™ã€‚å¾ˆé«˜å…´çŸ¥é“å¦‚ä½•ä»¥è¿™ç§æ–¹å¼è¿›è¡Œè¿æ¥ï¼Œä½†æ˜¯æˆ‘å¼ºçƒˆå»ºè®®ä½¿ç”¨ç¬¬äºŒç§æ–¹å¼ã€‚

```js
// Declaring different variables of different data types
let space = ' '
let firstName = 'Asabeneh'
let lastName = 'Yetayeh'
let country = 'Finland'
let city = 'Helsinki'
let language = 'JavaScript'
let job = 'teacher'
let age = 250
let fullName = firstName + space + lastName

let personInfoOne = fullName + '. I am ' + age + '. I live in ' + country; // ES5

console.log(personInfoOne)
```

```shell
Asabeneh Yetayeh. I am 250. I live in Finland
```

#### `Long Literal Strings`

å­—ç¬¦ä¸²å¯ä»¥æ˜¯å•ä¸ªå­—ç¬¦æˆ–æ®µè½æˆ–é¡µé¢ã€‚å¦‚æœå­—ç¬¦ä¸²é•¿åº¦å¤ªå¤§ï¼Œåˆ™ä¸èƒ½å®¹çº³ä¸€è¡Œã€‚æˆ‘ä»¬å¯ä»¥åœ¨æ¯ä¸€è¡Œçš„æœ«å°¾ä½¿ç”¨åæ–œæ å­—ç¬¦ï¼ˆ\\ï¼‰è¡¨ç¤ºè¯¥å­—ç¬¦ä¸²å°†åœ¨ä¸‹ä¸€è¡Œç»§ç»­ã€‚ **ä¾‹ï¼š** 

```js
const paragraph = "My name is Asabeneh Yetayeh. I live in Finland, Helsinki.\
I am a teacher and I love teaching. I teach HTML, CSS, JavaScript, React, Redux, \
Node.js, Python, Data Analysis and D3.js for anyone who is interested to learn. \
In the end of 2019, I was thinking to expand my teaching and to reach \
to global audience and I started a Python challenge from November 20 - December 19.\
It was one of the most rewarding and inspiring experience.\
Now, we are in 2020. I am enjoying preparing the 30DaysOfJavaScript challenge and \
I hope you are enjoying too."
console.log(paragraph)
```

#### `Escape Sequences in string`

åœ¨JavaScriptå’Œå…¶ä»–ç¼–ç¨‹è¯­è¨€ä¸­ï¼Œ\\åè·Ÿä¸€äº›å­—ç¬¦æ˜¯è½¬ä¹‰åºåˆ—ã€‚è®©æˆ‘ä»¬çœ‹çœ‹æœ€å¸¸è§çš„è½¬ä¹‰å­—ç¬¦ï¼š

*   \\ nï¼šæ–°è¡Œ
*   \\ tï¼šåˆ¶è¡¨ç¬¦ï¼ˆ8ä¸ªç©ºæ ¼ï¼‰
*   \\\\ï¼šåæ–œçº¿
*   \\'ï¼šå•å¼•å·ï¼ˆ'ï¼‰
*   \\â€œï¼šåŒå¼•å·ï¼ˆâ€ï¼‰

```js
console.log('I hope every one is enjoying the 30 Days Of JavaScript challenge.\nDo you ?') // line break
console.log('Days\tTopics\tExercises')
console.log('Day 1\t3\t5')
console.log('Day 2\t3\t5')
console.log('Day 3\t3\t5')
console.log('Day 4\t3\t5')
console.log('This is a back slash  symbol (\\)') // To write a back slash
console.log('In every programming language it starts with \"Hello, World!\"')
console.log("In every programming language it starts with \'Hello, World!\'")
console.log('The saying \'Seeing is Believing\' is\'t correct in 2020')
```

#### `Template Literals(Template Strings)`

è¦åˆ›å»ºæ¨¡æ¿å­—ç¬¦ä¸²ï¼Œæˆ‘ä»¬ä½¿ç”¨ä¸¤ä¸ªåå¼•å·ã€‚æˆ‘ä»¬å¯ä»¥å°†æ•°æ®ä½œä¸ºè¡¨è¾¾å¼æ’å…¥æ¨¡æ¿å­—ç¬¦ä¸²ä¸­ã€‚è¦æ³¨å…¥æ•°æ®ï¼Œæˆ‘ä»¬ç”¨å¤§æ‹¬å·ï¼ˆ{}ï¼‰åŠ ä¸Š$ç¬¦å·å°†è¡¨è¾¾å¼æ‹¬èµ·æ¥ã€‚è¯·å‚è§ä¸‹é¢çš„è¯­æ³•ã€‚

```js
//Syntax
`String literal text`
`String literal text ${expression}`
```

**èŒƒä¾‹ï¼š1**

```js
console.log(`The sum of 2 and 3 is 5`)              // statically writing the data
let a = 2
let b = 3
console.log(`The sum of ${a} and ${b} is ${a + b}`) // injecting the data dynamically
```

**ç¤ºä¾‹ï¼š2**

```js
let firstName = 'Asabeneh'
let lastName = 'Yetayeh'
let country = 'Finland'
let city = 'Helsinki'
let language = 'JavaScript'
let job = 'teacher'
let age = 250
let fullName = firstName + ' ' + lastName

let personInfoTwo = `I am ${fullName}. I am ${age}. I live in ${country}.` //ES6 - String interpolation method
let personInfoThree = `I am ${fullName}. I live in ${city}, ${country}. I am a ${job}. I teach ${language}.`
console.log(personInfoTwo)
console.log(personInfoThree)
```

```shell
I am Asabeneh Yetayeh. I am 250. I live in Finland.
I am Asabeneh Yetayeh. I live in Helsinki, Finland. I am a teacher. I teach JavaScript.
```

ä½¿ç”¨å­—ç¬¦ä¸²æ¨¡æ¿æˆ–å­—ç¬¦ä¸²æ’å€¼æ–¹æ³•ï¼Œæˆ‘ä»¬å¯ä»¥æ·»åŠ è¡¨è¾¾å¼ï¼Œå®ƒå¯ä»¥æ˜¯å€¼æˆ–æŸäº›è¿ç®—ï¼ˆæ¯”è¾ƒï¼Œç®—æœ¯è¿ç®—ï¼Œä¸‰å…ƒè¿ç®—ï¼‰ã€‚

```js
let a = 2
let b = 3
console.log(`${a} is greater than ${b}: ${a > b}`)
```

```shell
2 is greater than 3: false
```

### `String Methods`

JavaScriptä¸­çš„æ‰€æœ‰å†…å®¹éƒ½æ˜¯ä¸€ä¸ªå¯¹è±¡ã€‚å­—ç¬¦ä¸²æ˜¯ä¸€ç§åŸå§‹æ•°æ®ç±»å‹ï¼Œè¿™æ„å‘³ç€ä¸€æ—¦åˆ›å»ºå®ƒå°±æ— æ³•ä¿®æ”¹ã€‚å­—ç¬¦ä¸²å¯¹è±¡æœ‰è®¸å¤šå­—ç¬¦ä¸²æ–¹æ³•ã€‚æœ‰å¤šç§å­—ç¬¦ä¸²æ–¹æ³•å¯ä»¥å¸®åŠ©æˆ‘ä»¬å¤„ç†å­—ç¬¦ä¸²ã€‚

1.  _length_ï¼šå­—ç¬¦ä¸²_é•¿åº¦_æ–¹æ³•è¿”å›åŒ…å«ç©ºæ ¼çš„å­—ç¬¦ä¸²ä¸­çš„å­—ç¬¦æ•°ã€‚ **ä¾‹ï¼š** 
    
    ```js
    let js = 'JavaScript'
    console.log(js.length)         // 10
    let firstName = 'Asabeneh'
    console.log(firstName.length)  // 8
    ```
    
2.  _è®¿é—®å­—ç¬¦ä¸²ä¸­çš„å­—ç¬¦_ï¼šæˆ‘ä»¬å¯ä»¥ä½¿ç”¨å…¶ç´¢å¼•è®¿é—®å­—ç¬¦ä¸²ä¸­çš„æ¯ä¸ªå­—ç¬¦ã€‚åœ¨ç¼–ç¨‹ä¸­ï¼Œè®¡æ•°ä»0å¼€å§‹ã€‚å­—ç¬¦ä¸²çš„ç¬¬ä¸€ä¸ªç´¢å¼•ä¸ºé›¶ï¼Œæœ€åä¸€ä¸ªç´¢å¼•ä¸º1å‡å»å­—ç¬¦ä¸²çš„é•¿åº¦ã€‚
    

[![](https://github.com/Asabeneh/JavaScript-for-Everyone/raw/master/images/string_indexes.png)
](https://github.com/Asabeneh/JavaScript-for-Everyone/blob/master/images/string_indexes.png)

è®©æˆ‘ä»¬è®¿é—®â€œ JavaScriptâ€å­—ç¬¦ä¸²ä¸­çš„ä¸åŒå­—ç¬¦ã€‚

```js
let string = 'JavaScript'
let firstLetter = string[0]

console.log(firstLetter)           // J

let secondLetter = string[1]       // a
let thirdLetter = string[2]
let lastLetter = string[9]

console.log(lastLetter)            // t

let lastIndex = string.length - 1

console.log(lastIndex)  // 9
console.log(string[lastIndex])    // t
```

3.  _toUpperCaseï¼ˆï¼‰_ï¼šæ­¤æ–¹æ³•å°†å­—ç¬¦ä¸²æ›´æ”¹ä¸ºå¤§å†™å­—æ¯ã€‚

```js
let string = 'JavaScript'

console.log(string.toUpperCase())     // JAVASCRIPT

let firstName = 'Asabeneh'

console.log(firstName.toUpperCase())  // ASABENEH

let country = 'Finland'

console.log(country.toUpperCase())    // FINLAND
```

4.  _toLowerCaseï¼ˆï¼‰_ï¼šæ­¤æ–¹æ³•å°†å­—ç¬¦ä¸²æ›´æ”¹ä¸ºå°å†™å­—æ¯ã€‚

```js
let string = 'JavasCript'

console.log(string.toLowerCase())     // javascript

let firstName = 'Asabeneh'

console.log(firstName.toLowerCase())  // asabeneh

let country = 'Finland'

console.log(country.toLowerCase())   // finland
```

5.  _substrï¼ˆï¼‰_ï¼šå®ƒæœ‰ä¸¤ä¸ªå‚æ•°ï¼Œèµ·å§‹ç´¢å¼•å’Œè¦åˆ†å‰²çš„å­—ç¬¦æ•°ã€‚

```js
let string = 'JavaScript'
console.log(string.substr(4,6))    // Script

let country = 'Finland'
console.log(country.substr(3, 4))   // land
```

6.  _substringï¼ˆï¼‰_ï¼šå®ƒæœ‰ä¸¤ä¸ªå‚æ•°ï¼Œèµ·å§‹ç´¢å¼•å’Œç»ˆæ­¢ç´¢å¼•ï¼Œä½†ä¸åŒ…å«ç»ˆæ­¢ç´¢å¼•ã€‚

```js
let string = 'JavaScript'

console.log(string.substring(0,4))     // Java
console.log(string.substring(4,10))    // Script
console.log(string.substring(4))       // Script

let country = 'Finland'

console.log(country.substring(0, 3))   // Fin
console.log(country.substring(3, 7))   // land
console.log(country.substring(3))      // land
```

7.  _splitï¼ˆï¼‰_ï¼šsplitæ–¹æ³•åœ¨æŒ‡å®šä½ç½®åˆ†å‰²å­—ç¬¦ä¸²ã€‚

```js
let string = '30 Days Of JavaScript'

console.log(string.split())     // ["30 Days Of JavaScript"]
console.log(string.split(' '))  // ["30", "Days", "Of", "JavaScript"]

let firstName = 'Asabeneh'

console.log(firstName.split())    // ["Asabeneh"]
console.log(firstName.split(''))  // ["A", "s", "a", "b", "e", "n", "e", "h"]

let countries = 'Finland, Sweden, Norway, Denmark, and Iceland'

console.log(countries.split(','))  // ["Finland", " Sweden", " Norway", " Denmark", " and Iceland"]
console.log(countries.split(', ')) //  ["Finland", "Sweden", "Norway", "Denmark", "and Iceland"]
```

8.  _trimï¼ˆï¼‰_ï¼šåˆ é™¤å­—ç¬¦ä¸²å¼€å¤´æˆ–ç»“å°¾çš„å°¾éƒ¨ç©ºæ ¼ã€‚

```js
let string = '   30 Days Of JavaScript   '

console.log(string)     
console.log(string.trim(' '))

let firstName = ' Asabeneh '

console.log(firstName)
console.log(firstName.trim())
```

```shell
   30 Days Of JavasCript   
30 Days Of JavasCript
  Asabeneh 
Asabeneh
```

9.  _includeï¼ˆï¼‰_ï¼šå®ƒæ¥å—ä¸€ä¸ªå­å­—ç¬¦ä¸²å‚æ•°ï¼Œå¹¶æ£€æŸ¥å­—ç¬¦ä¸²ä¸­æ˜¯å¦å­˜åœ¨å­å­—ç¬¦ä¸²å‚æ•°ã€‚_includeï¼ˆï¼‰_è¿”å›ä¸€ä¸ªå¸ƒå°”å€¼ã€‚å®ƒæ£€æŸ¥å­—ç¬¦ä¸²ä¸­æ˜¯å¦å­˜åœ¨å­å­—ç¬¦ä¸²ï¼Œå¦‚æœå­˜åœ¨åˆ™è¿”å›trueï¼Œå¦‚æœä¸å­˜åœ¨åˆ™è¿”å›falseã€‚

```js
let string = '30 Days Of JavaScript'

console.log(string.includes('Days'))     // true
console.log(string.includes('days'))     // false
console.log(string.includes('Script'))   // true
console.log(string.includes('script'))   // false
console.log(string.includes('java'))     // false
console.log(string.includes('Java'))     // true

let country = 'Finland'

console.log(country.includes('fin'))     // false
console.log(country.includes('Fin'))     // true
console.log(country.includes('land'))    // true
console.log(country.includes('Land'))    // false
```

10.  _replaceï¼ˆï¼‰_ï¼šå°†æ—§å­å­—ç¬¦ä¸²å’Œæ–°å­å­—ç¬¦ä¸²ä½œä¸ºå‚æ•°ã€‚

```js
string.replace(oldsubstring, newsubstring)
```

```js
let string = '30 Days Of JavaScript'
console.log(string.replace('JavaScript', 'Python')) // 30 Days Of Python

let country = 'Finland'
console.log(country.replace('Fin', 'Noman'))       // Nomanland
```

11.  _charAtï¼ˆï¼‰_ï¼šè·å–ç´¢å¼•ï¼Œå¹¶è¿”å›è¯¥ç´¢å¼•å¤„çš„å€¼

```js

let lastIndex = string.length - 1
console.log(string.charAt(lastIndex)) // t
```

12.  _charCodeAtï¼ˆï¼‰_ï¼šè·å–ç´¢å¼•ï¼Œå¹¶è¿”å›è¯¥ç´¢å¼•å¤„çš„å€¼çš„charç ï¼ˆASCIIç ï¼‰

```js

console.log(string.charCodeAt(lastIndex)) // t ASCII is 116
```

13.  _indexOfï¼ˆï¼‰_ï¼šè·å–ä¸€ä¸ªå­å­—ç¬¦ä¸²ï¼Œå¦‚æœè¯¥å­å­—ç¬¦ä¸²å­˜åœ¨äºå­—ç¬¦ä¸²ä¸­ï¼Œåˆ™è¿”å›å­å­—ç¬¦ä¸²çš„ç¬¬ä¸€ä¸ªä½ç½®ï¼›å¦‚æœä¸å­˜åœ¨ï¼Œåˆ™è¿”å›-1

```js

```

```js

console.log(string.indexOf('Days'))       // 3

console.log(string.indexOf('a'))          // 4
console.log(string.indexOf('JavaScript')) // 11
console.log(string.indexOf('Script'))     //15
console.log(string.indexOf('script'))     // -1
```

14.  _lastIndexOfï¼ˆï¼‰_ï¼šè·å–ä¸€ä¸ªå­å­—ç¬¦ä¸²ï¼Œå¦‚æœè¯¥å­å­—ç¬¦ä¸²å­˜åœ¨äºå­—ç¬¦ä¸²ä¸­ï¼Œåˆ™è¿”å›è¯¥å­å­—ç¬¦ä¸²çš„æœ€åä½ç½®ï¼›å¦‚æœä¸å­˜åœ¨ï¼Œåˆ™è¿”å›-1


```js

console.log(string.lastIndexOf('you'))        // 63
console.log(string.lastIndexOf('JavaScript')) // 38
```

15.  _concatï¼ˆï¼‰_ï¼šå®ƒéœ€è¦è®¸å¤šå­å­—ç¬¦ä¸²å¹¶åˆ›å»ºä¸²è”ã€‚


```js

```

16.  _startsWith_ï¼šå®ƒå°†å­å­—ç¬¦ä¸²ä½œä¸ºå‚æ•°ï¼Œå¹¶æ£€æŸ¥å­—ç¬¦ä¸²æ˜¯å¦ä»¥æŒ‡å®šçš„å­å­—ç¬¦ä¸²å¼€å¤´ã€‚å®ƒè¿”å›ä¸€ä¸ªå¸ƒå°”å€¼ï¼ˆtrueæˆ–falseï¼‰ã€‚

```js
//syntax

```

```js

console.log(string.startsWith('love'))   // false
console.log(string.startsWith('world'))  // false

console.log(country.startsWith('Fin'))   // true
console.log(country.startsWith('fin'))   // false
console.log(country.startsWith('land'))  //  false
```

17.  _EndsWith_ï¼šå®ƒå°†å­å­—ç¬¦ä¸²ä½œä¸ºå‚æ•°ï¼Œå¹¶æ£€æŸ¥å­—ç¬¦ä¸²æ˜¯å¦ä»¥æŒ‡å®šçš„å­å­—ç¬¦ä¸²å¼€å¤´ã€‚å®ƒè¿”å›ä¸€ä¸ªå¸ƒå°”å€¼ï¼ˆtrueæˆ–falseï¼‰ã€‚


```js

```

18.  _search_ï¼šå°†å­å­—ç¬¦ä¸²ä½œä¸ºå‚æ•°ï¼Œå¹¶è¿”å›ç¬¬ä¸€ä¸ªåŒ¹é…é¡¹çš„ç´¢å¼•ã€‚

```js

```

19.  _match_ï¼šå®ƒå°†å­å­—ç¬¦ä¸²æˆ–æ­£åˆ™è¡¨è¾¾å¼æ¨¡å¼ä½œä¸ºå‚æ•°ï¼Œå¦‚æœåŒ¹é…åˆ™è¿”å›æ•°ç»„ï¼Œå¦åˆ™è¿”å›nullã€‚è®©æˆ‘ä»¬çœ‹çœ‹æ­£åˆ™è¡¨è¾¾å¼æ¨¡å¼çš„æ ·å­ã€‚å®ƒä»¥/ç¬¦å·å¼€å¤´ï¼Œä»¥/ç¬¦å·ç»“å°¾ã€‚

```js
let string = 'love'
let patternOne = /love/     // with out any flag
let patternTwo = /love/gi   // g-means to search in the whole text, i - case insensitive
```

åŒ¹é…è¯­æ³•

```js
// syntax
string.match(substring)
```

```js
let string = 'I love JavaScript. If you do not love JavaScript what else can you love.'
console.log(string.match('love'))
```

```shell
["love", index: 2, input: "I love JavaScript. If you do not love JavaScript what else can you love.", groups: undefined]
```

```js
let pattern = /love/gi
console.log(string.match(pattern))   // ["love", "love", "love"]
```

è®©æˆ‘ä»¬ä½¿ç”¨æ­£åˆ™è¡¨è¾¾å¼ä»æ–‡æœ¬ä¸­æå–æ•°å­—ã€‚è¿™ä¸æ˜¯æ­£åˆ™è¡¨è¾¾å¼éƒ¨åˆ†ï¼Œæ²¡æœ‰ææ…Œï¼Œæˆ‘ä»¬å°†åœ¨å…¶ä»–éƒ¨åˆ†ä»‹ç»æ­£åˆ™è¡¨è¾¾å¼ã€‚

```js
let txt = 'In 2019, I run 30 Days of Python. Now, in 2020 I super exited to start this challenge'
let regEx = /\d+/

// d with escape character means d not a normal d instead acts a digit
// + means one or more digit numbers,
// if there is g after that it means global, search everywhere.

console.log(txt.match(regEx))  // ["2", "0", "1", "9", "3", "0", "2", "0", "2", "0"]
console.log(txt.match(/\d+/g)) // ["2019", "30", "2020"]
```

20.  _repeatï¼ˆï¼‰_ï¼šæ¥å—æ•°å­—å‚æ•°ï¼Œå¹¶è¿”å›å­—ç¬¦ä¸²çš„é‡å¤ç‰ˆæœ¬ã€‚

```js
let string = 'love'
console.log(string.repeat(10)) // lovelovelovelovelovelovelovelovelovelove
```

`Checking Data types and Casting`
---------------------------------

### `Checking data types`

*   æ£€æŸ¥æ•°æ®ç±»å‹ï¼šè¦æ£€æŸ¥æŸç§æ•°æ®ç±»å‹çš„æ•°æ®ç±»å‹ï¼Œæˆ‘ä»¬ä½¿ç”¨_typeof_ï¼Œå¹¶ä¸”è¿˜å°†ä¸€ç§æ•°æ®ç±»å‹æ›´æ”¹ä¸ºå¦ä¸€ç§ã€‚ **ä¾‹ï¼š** 

```js
// Different javascript data types
// Let's declare different data types

let firstName = 'Asabeneh'      // string
let lastName = 'Yetayeh'        // string
let country = 'Finland'         // string
let city = 'Helsinki'           // string
let age = 250                   // number, it is not my real age, do not worry about it
let job                         // undefined, because a value was not assigned

console.log(typeof 'Asabeneh')  // string
console.log(typeof firstName)   // string
console.log(typeof 10)          // number
console.log(typeof 3.14)        // number
console.log(typeof true)        // boolean
console.log(typeof false)       // boolean
console.log(typeof NaN)         // number
console.log(typeof job)         // undefined
console.log(typeof undefined)   // undefined
console.log(typeof null)        // object
```

### `Changing data type(Casting)`

*   è½¬æ¢ï¼šå°†ä¸€ç§æ•°æ®ç±»å‹è½¬æ¢ä¸ºå¦ä¸€ç§æ•°æ®ç±»å‹ã€‚æˆ‘ä»¬ä½¿ç”¨_parseIntï¼ˆï¼‰_ï¼Œ_parseFloatï¼ˆï¼‰_ï¼Œ_Numberï¼ˆï¼‰_ï¼Œ_+å·_ï¼Œ_strï¼ˆï¼‰_ è¿›è¡Œç®—æœ¯è¿ç®—æ—¶ï¼Œåº”é¦–å…ˆå°†å­—ç¬¦ä¸²æ•°å­—è½¬æ¢ä¸ºæ•´æ•°æˆ–æµ®ç‚¹æ•°ï¼Œå¦åˆ™å°†è¿”å›é”™è¯¯ã€‚

#### `String to Int`

æˆ‘ä»¬å¯ä»¥å°†å­—ç¬¦ä¸²å·è½¬æ¢ä¸ºæ•°å­—ã€‚å¼•å·å†…çš„ä»»ä½•æ•°å­—éƒ½æ˜¯å­—ç¬¦ä¸²ã€‚å­—ç¬¦ä¸²æ•°å­—çš„ç¤ºä¾‹ï¼šâ€œ 10â€ï¼Œâ€œ 5â€ç­‰ã€‚æˆ‘ä»¬å¯ä»¥ä½¿ç”¨ä»¥ä¸‹æ–¹æ³•å°†å­—ç¬¦ä¸²è½¬æ¢ä¸ºæ•°å­—ï¼š

*   parseIntï¼ˆï¼‰
*   æ•°ï¼ˆï¼‰
*   åŠ å·ï¼ˆ+ï¼‰

```js
let num = '10'
let numInt = parseInt(num)
console.log(numInt) // 10
```

```js
let num = '10'
let numInt = Number(num)

console.log(numInt) // 10
```

```js
let num = '10'
let numInt = +num

console.log(numInt) // 10
```

#### `String to Float`

æˆ‘ä»¬å¯ä»¥å°†å­—ç¬¦ä¸²æµ®ç‚¹æ•°è½¬æ¢ä¸ºæµ®ç‚¹æ•°ã€‚å¼•å·å†…çš„ä»»ä½•æµ®ç‚¹æ•°éƒ½æ˜¯å­—ç¬¦ä¸²æµ®ç‚¹æ•°ã€‚å­—ç¬¦ä¸²æµ®ç‚¹æ•°çš„ç¤ºä¾‹ï¼š'9.81'ï¼Œ'3.14'ï¼Œ'1.44'ç­‰ã€‚æˆ‘ä»¬å¯ä»¥ä½¿ç”¨ä»¥ä¸‹æ–¹æ³•å°†å­—ç¬¦ä¸²æµ®ç‚¹æ•°è½¬æ¢ä¸ºæ•°å­—ï¼š

*   parseFloatï¼ˆï¼‰
*   æ•°ï¼ˆï¼‰
*   åŠ å·ï¼ˆ+ï¼‰

```js
let num = '9.81'
let numFloat = parseFloat(num)

console.log(numFloat) // 9.81
```

```js
let num = '9.81'
let numFloat = Number(num)

console.log(numFloat) // 9.81
```

```js
let num = '9.81'
let numFloat = +num

console.log(numInt) // 9.81
```

#### `Float to Int`

æˆ‘ä»¬å¯ä»¥å°†æµ®ç‚¹æ•°è½¬æ¢ä¸ºæ•´æ•°ã€‚æˆ‘ä»¬ä½¿ç”¨ä»¥ä¸‹æ–¹æ³•å°†floatè½¬æ¢ä¸ºintï¼š

*   parseIntï¼ˆï¼‰

```js
let num = 9.81
let numInt = parseInt(num)

console.log(numInt) // 9
```

### `Booleans`

å¸ƒå°”å€¼æ˜¯trueæˆ–falseã€‚ä»»ä½•æ¯”è¾ƒéƒ½ä¼šè¿”å›ä¸€ä¸ªå¸ƒå°”å€¼ï¼Œè¯¥å¸ƒå°”å€¼å¯ä»¥ä¸ºtrueæˆ–falseã€‚

#### `Exercise: Booleans`

å¸ƒå°”å€¼æ˜¯trueæˆ–falseã€‚

### `Undefined`

```js
let firstName;
console.log(firstName); //not defined, because it is not assigned to a value yet
```

### `Null`

```js
let empty = null;
console.log(empty); // -> null , means no value
```

### `Exercise - 6 : Data types`

å­—ç¬¦ä¸²ï¼Œæ•°å­—ï¼Œå¸ƒå°”å€¼ï¼Œnullï¼Œæœªå®šä¹‰å’Œsymbolï¼ˆES6ï¼‰æ˜¯JavaScriptåŸºæœ¬æ•°æ®ç±»å‹ã€‚

1.  JavaScript _typeof_è¿ç®—ç¬¦ç”¨äºæ£€æŸ¥ä¸åŒçš„æ•°æ®ç±»å‹ã€‚æ£€æŸ¥é—®é¢˜ç¼–å·1ä¸­æ¯ä¸ªå˜é‡çš„æ•°æ®ç±»å‹ã€‚

`Operators`
-----------

### `Arithmetic Operators`

ç®—æœ¯è¿ç®—ç¬¦æ˜¯æ•°å­¦è¿ç®—ç¬¦ï¼š+ï¼Œ-ï¼Œ\_ï¼Œ/ï¼Œ\_

```js
let numOne = 4;
let numTwo = 3;
let sum = numOne + numTwo;
let diff = numOne - numTwo;
let mult = numOne * numTwo;
let div = numOne / numTwo;
let remainder = numOne % numTwo;

console.log(sum, diff, mult, div, remainder); // ->7,1,12,1.33,1

let PI = 3.14;
let radius = 100;          // length in meter

const gravity = 9.81;      // in m/s2
let mass = 72;             // in Kilogram
const boilingPoint = 100;  // temperature in oC, boiling point of water
const bodyTemp = 37;       // body temperature in oC

// Lets calculate area of a circle

const areaOfCircle = PI * radius * radius;
console.log(areaOfCircle); // -> 314 m

// Lets calculate weight of a substance
const weight = mass * gravity;
console.log(weight); // -> 706.32 N(Newton)

// ConcatEnating string with numbers using string interpolation
/*
 The boiling point of water is 100 oC.
 Human body temperature is 37 oC.
 The gravity of earth is 9.81 m/s2.
 */
console.log(
  `The boiling point of water is ${boilingPoint} oC.\nHuman body temperature is ${body} oC.\nThe gravity of earth is ${gravity} m / s2.`
);
```

### `Logical Operators`

ä»¥ä¸‹ç¬¦å·æ˜¯å¸¸è§çš„é€»è¾‘è¿ç®—ç¬¦ï¼š&&ï¼ˆï¼†ï¼‰å’Œ||ï¼ˆpipeï¼‰å’Œï¼ï¼ˆnegationï¼‰ã€‚&&ä»…å½“ä¸¤ä¸ªæ“ä½œæ•°ä¸ºtrueæ—¶æ‰ä¸ºtrueã€‚|| å¾—åˆ°çœŸï¼Œå…¶ä¸­ä»»ä½•ä¸€ä¸ªæ“ä½œæ•°éƒ½ä¸ºçœŸã€‚ï¼å¦å®šçœŸå‡ï¼Œå‡çœŸã€‚

```js
// && ampersand example

const check = 4 > 3 && 10 > 5; // true and true -> true
const check = 4 > 3 && 10 < 5; // true and false -> false
const check = 4 < 3 && 10 < 5; // false and false -> false

// || pipe or, example

const check = 4 > 3 || 10 > 5; // true and true -> true
const check = 4 > 3 || 10 < 5; // true and false -> true
const check = 4 < 3 || 10 < 5; // false and false -> false

// ! Negation examples

let check = 4 > 3;           // -> true
let check = !(4 > 3);        // -> false
let isLightOn = true;        // -> true
let isLightOff = !isLightOn; // -> false
let isMarried = !false;      // -> true
```

`Conditionals`
--------------

### `if`

æˆ‘ä»¬ä½¿ç”¨ifæ¡ä»¶åªæ£€æŸ¥æ¡ä»¶ã€‚

```js
if (condition) {
  // code goes here
}

let isRaining = true;
if (isRaining) {
  console.log('Remember to take your rain coat.');
}
```

### `if else`

å½“æˆ‘ä»¬æœ‰å¤šä¸ªæ¡ä»¶æ—¶ï¼Œæˆ‘ä»¬ä½¿ç”¨ifå’Œelseæ¡ä»¶ã€‚

```js
if (condition) {
  // if the condition meets, this block of code runs
} else {
  // if condition doesn't meet, this block code runs
}

let isRaining = true;
if (isRaining) {
  console.log('You need a rain coat.');
} else {
  console.log('No need for a rain coat.');
}
```

### `if else if else`

æ¯å½“æˆ‘ä»¬æœ‰å¤šä¸ªæ¡ä»¶æ—¶ã€‚

```js
// if else if else
let weather = 'sunny';
if (weather === 'rainy') {
  console.log('You need a rain coat.');
} else if (weather === 'cloudy') {
  console.log('It might be cold, you need a jacket.');
} else if (weather === 'sunny') {
  console.log('Go out freely.');
} else {
  console.log('No need for rain coat.');
}
```

### `switch`

å¦‚æœä¸æ˜¯ï¼Œåˆ™åˆ‡æ¢å…¶ä»–é€‰é¡¹

```js
var weather = 'cloudy';
switch (weather) {
  case 'rainy':
    console.log('You need a rain coat.');
    break;
  case 'cloudy':
    console.log('It might be cold, you need a jacket.');
    break;
  case 'sunny':
    console.log('Go out freely.');
    break;
  default:
    console.log(' No need for rain coat.');
    break;
}
// Switch More Examples
var dayUserInput = prompt('What day is it ?');
var day = dayUserInput.toLowerCase();
switch (day) {
  case 'monday':
    console.log('Today is Monday');
    break;
  case 'tuesday':
    console.log('Today is Tuesday');
    break;
  case 'wednesday':
    console.log('Today is Wednesday');
    break;
  case 'thursday':
    console.log('Today is Thursday');
    break;
  case 'friday':
    console.log('Today is Friday');
    break;
  case 'saturday':
    console.log('Today is Saturday');
    break;
  case 'sunday':
    console.log('Today is Sunday');
    break;

  default:
    console.log('It is not a week day.');
    break;
}
```

### `Ternary Operators`

ç¼–å†™æ¡ä»¶è¯­å¥çš„å¦ä¸€ç§æ–¹æ³•æ˜¯ä½¿ç”¨ä¸‰å…ƒè¿ç®—ç¬¦ã€‚

```js
let isRaining = true;
isRaining
  ? console.log('You need a rain coat.')
  : console.log('No need for a rain coat.');
```

`Loops`
-------

åœ¨æ‰§è¡Œé‡å¤æ€§ä»»åŠ¡çš„ç¼–ç¨‹è¯­è¨€ä¸­ï¼Œæˆ‘ä»¬ä½¿ç”¨ä¸åŒç§ç±»çš„å¾ªç¯ã€‚ä»¥ä¸‹ç¤ºä¾‹æ˜¯å¸¸ç”¨çš„å¾ªç¯ã€‚

### `For Loop`

```js
// for loop structure
for(initialization, condition, increment/decrement){
  // code goes here
}
for(let i = 0; i <= 5; i++){
  console.log(i)
}
```

### `While loop`

```js
let i = 0;
while (i <= 5) {
  console.log(i);
  i++;
}
```

### `Do while loop`

```js
let i = 0;
do {
  console.log(i);
  i++;
} while (i <= 5);
```

`Arrays`
--------

ä¸å˜é‡ç›¸åï¼Œæ•°ç»„å¯ä»¥å­˜å‚¨_å¤šä¸ªå€¼_ã€‚æ•°ç»„ä¸­çš„æ¯ä¸ªå€¼éƒ½æœ‰ä¸€ä¸ª_ç´¢å¼•ï¼Œ_è€Œæ¯ä¸ªç´¢å¼•_åœ¨å†…å­˜åœ°å€ä¸­_éƒ½æœ‰_ä¸€ä¸ªå¼•ç”¨_ã€‚æ¯ä¸ªå€¼éƒ½å¯ä»¥ä½¿ç”¨å…¶_ç´¢å¼•_è¿›è¡Œè®¿é—®ã€‚æ•°ç»„çš„ç´¢å¼•_ä»é›¶å¼€å§‹_ï¼Œæœ€åä¸€ä¸ªå…ƒç´ æ¯”æ•°ç»„çš„é•¿åº¦å°‘ä¸€ã€‚

```js
const numbers = [0, 3.14, 9.81, 37, 98.6, 100]; // set of numbers

console.log(numbers.length) // => to know the size of the array, which is 6
console.log(numbers)        // -> [0, 3.14, 9.81, 37, 98.6, 100]
console.log(numbers[0])     //  -> 0
console.log(numbers[5])     //  -> 100

let lastIndex = numbers.length - 1;
console.log(numbers[lastIndex]) -> 100
const webTechs = [
  'HTML',
  'CSS',
  'JavaScript',
  'React',
  'Redux',
  'Node',
  'MongoDB'
]; // List of web technologies

console.log(webTechs)        // all the array items
console.log(webTechs.length) // => to know the size of the array, which is 7
console.log(webTechs[0])     //  -> HTML
console.log(webTechs[6])     //  -> MongoDB

let lastIndex = webTechs.length - 1;
console.log(webTechs[lastIndex]) -> MongoDB
const countries = [
  'Albania',
  'Bolivia',
  'Canada',
  'Denmark',
  'Ethiopia',
  'Finland',
  'Germany',
  'Hungary',
  'Ireland',
  'Japan',
  'Kenya'
]; // List of countries;

console.log(countries)     // -> all countries in array
console.log(countries[0])  //  -> Albania
console.log(countries[10]) //  -> Kenya

let lastIndex = countries.length - 1;
console.log(countries[lastIndex]) -> // Kenya

const shoppingCart = [
  'Milk',
  'Mango',
  'Tomato',
  'Potato',
  'Avocado',
  'Meat',
  'Eggs',
  'Sugar'
]; // List of food products

console.log(shoppingCart)     // -> all shoppingCart in array
console.log(shoppingCart[0])  //  -> Milk
console.log(shoppingCart[7])  //  -> Sugar

let lastIndex = shoppingCart.length - 1;
console.log(shoppingCart[lastIndex]) -> // Sugar
```

`More on Arrays`
----------------

æœ‰å¤šç§æ“ä½œæ•°ç»„çš„æ–¹æ³•ã€‚è¿™äº›æ˜¯å¤„ç†æ•°ç»„çš„ä¸€äº›å¯ç”¨æ–¹æ³•ï¼š_Arrayï¼Œlengthï¼Œconcatï¼ŒindexOfï¼Œsliceï¼Œspliceï¼Œjoinï¼ŒtoStringï¼Œincludesï¼ŒlastIndexOfï¼ŒisArrayï¼Œfillï¼Œpushï¼Œpopï¼Œshiftï¼Œunshift_ Arrayï¼šåˆ›å»ºæ•°ç»„ã€‚

```js
const arr = Array(); // creates an an empty array
console.log(arr);

const eightEmptyValues = Array(8); // it creates eight empty values
console.log(eightEmptyValues);     // [empty x 8]
```

*   _fill_ï¼šç”¨é™æ€å€¼å¡«å……æ‰€æœ‰æ•°ç»„å…ƒç´ 

```js
const arr = Array();                     // creates an an empty array
console.log(arr);
const eightXvalues = Array(8).fill('X'); // it creates eight element values
console.log(eightXvalues);               // ['X', 'X','X','X','X','X','X','X']
```

*   _concat_ï¼šè¿æ¥ä¸¤ä¸ªæ•°ç»„ã€‚

```js
const firstList = [1, 2, 3];
const secondList = [4, 5, 6];
const thirdList = firstList.concat(secondList);

console.log(thirdList); // [1,2,3,4,5,6]
```

*   _é•¿åº¦_ï¼šè¦çŸ¥é“æ•°ç»„çš„å¤§å°

```js
const numbers = [1, 2, 3, 4, 5];
console.log(numbers.length); // -> 5
```

*   _indexOf_ï¼šæ£€æŸ¥æ•°ç»„ä¸­æ˜¯å¦å­˜åœ¨é¡¹ã€‚å¦‚æœå­˜åœ¨ï¼Œåˆ™è¿”å›ç´¢å¼•ï¼Œå¦åˆ™è¿”å›-1ã€‚

```js
const numbers = [1, 2, 3, 4, 5];

console.log(numbers.indexOf(5));  // -> 4
console.log(numbers.indexOf(0));  // -> -1
console.log(numbers.indexOf(1));  // -> 0
console.log(numbers.indexOf(6));  // -> -1
```

*   _lastIndexOf_ï¼šç»™å‡ºæ•°ç»„ä¸­æœ€åä¸€é¡¹çš„ä½ç½®ã€‚å¦‚æœå­˜åœ¨ï¼Œåˆ™è¿”å›ç´¢å¼•ï¼Œå¦åˆ™è¿”å›-1ã€‚

```js
const numbers = [1, 2, 3, 4, 5, 3, 1, 2];

console.log(numbers.lastIndexOf(2));  // -> 7
console.log(numbers.lastIndexOf(0));  // -> -1
console.log(numbers.lastIndexOf(1));  // -> 6
console.log(numbers.lastIndexOf(4));  // -> 3
console.log(numbers.lastIndexOf(6));  // -> -1
```

_åŒ…æ‹¬_ï¼šæ£€æŸ¥é¡¹ç›®æ˜¯å¦å­˜åœ¨äºæ•°ç»„ä¸­ã€‚å¦‚æœå­˜åœ¨ï¼Œåˆ™è¿”å›trueï¼Œå¦åˆ™è¿”å›falseã€‚

```js
const numbers = [1, 2, 3, 4, 5];

console.log(numbers.includes(5)); // -> true
console.log(numbers.includes(0)); // -> false
console.log(numbers.includes(1)); // -> true
console.log(numbers.includes(6)); // -> false
```

*   _isArray_ï¼šæ£€æŸ¥æ•°æ®ç±»å‹æ˜¯å¦ä¸ºæ•°ç»„

```js
const numbers = [1, 2, 3, 4, 5];
console.log(Array.isArray(numbers)); // -> true

const number = 100;
console.log(Array.isArray(number)); // -> false
```

*   _toString_ï¼šå°†æ•°ç»„è½¬æ¢ä¸ºå­—ç¬¦ä¸²

```js
const numbers = [1, 2, 3, 4, 5];
console.log(numbers.toString()); // 1,2,3,4,5

const names = ['Asabeneh', 'Mathias', 'Elias', 'Brook'];
console.log(names.toString()); // Asabeneh,Mathias,Elias,Brook
```

joinï¼šè¦è¿æ¥æ•°ç»„ä¸­çš„å…ƒç´ ï¼Œåœ¨joinæ–¹æ³•ä¸­ä¼ é€’çš„å‚æ•°å°†è¢«è¿æ¥åˆ°æ•°ç»„ä¸­å¹¶ä½œä¸ºå­—ç¬¦ä¸²è¿”å›ã€‚

```js
const numbers = [1, 2, 3, 4, 5];
console.log(numbers.join());        // 1,2,3,4,5
const names = ['Asabeneh', 'Mathias', 'Elias', 'Brook'];
console.log(names.join());          // Asabeneh,Mathias,Elias,Brook
console.log(names.join(''));        //AsabenehMathiasEliasBrook
console.log(names.join(' '));       //Asabeneh Mathias Elias Brook
console.log(names.join(', '));      //Asabeneh, Mathias, Elias, Brook
console.log(names.join(' # '));     //Asabeneh # Mathias # Elias # Brook
```

åˆ‡ç‰‡ï¼šåˆ‡å‡ºèŒƒå›´å†…çš„å¤šä¸ªé¡¹ç›®ã€‚å®ƒæœ‰ä¸¤ä¸ªå‚æ•°ï¼šå¼€å§‹ä½ç½®å’Œç»“æŸä½ç½®ã€‚ä¸åŒ…æ‹¬ç»“æŸä½ç½®

```js
  const numbers = [1,2,3,4,5];
  console.log(numbers.slice()        // -> it copies all  item
  console.log(numbers.slice(0)       // -> it copies all  item
  console.log(numbers.indexOf(0, numbers.length)) // it copies all  item
  console.log(numbers.slice(1,4))    // -> [2,3,4] // it doesn't include the ending position
```

æ¥å¤´ï¼šå®ƒåŒ…å«ä¸‰ä¸ªå‚æ•°ï¼šèµ·å§‹ä½ç½®ï¼Œè¦åˆ é™¤çš„æ¬¡æ•°å’Œè¦æ·»åŠ çš„é¡¹ç›®ã€‚

```js
  const numbers = [1, 2, 3, 4, 5];
  console.log(numbers.splice()      // -> remove all items
  console.log(numbers.splice(0,1))  // remove the first item
  console.log(numbers.splice(3, 3, 6, 7, 8)) // -> [1,2,6,7,8] //it removes two item and replace three items
```

*   _æ¨é€_ï¼šæœ€åæ·»åŠ é¡¹ç›®

```js
const numbers = [1, 2, 3, 4, 5];
numbers.push(6);

console.log(numbers);  // -> [1,2,3,4,5,6]

numbers.pop();         // -> remove one item from the end
console.log(numbers);  // -> [1,2,3,4,5]
```

*   _pop_ï¼šæœ€ååˆ é™¤é¡¹ç›®

```js
const numbers = [1, 2, 3, 4, 5];
numbers.pop(); // -> remove one item from the end

console.log(numbers); // -> [1,2,3,4]
```

*   _shift_ï¼šå¼€å¤´åˆ é™¤é¡¹ç›®

```js
const numbers = [1, 2, 3, 4, 5];
numbers.shift(); // -> remove one item from the beginning

console.log(numbers); // -> [2,3,4,5]
```

*   _unshift_ï¼šåœ¨å¼€å¤´æ·»åŠ é¡¹ç›®

```js
const numbers = [1, 2, 3, 4, 5];
numbers.unshift(0);             // -> remove one item from the beginning
console.log(numbers);           // -> [0,1,2,3,4,5]
```

`Functions`
-----------

å‡½æ•°æ˜¯æ—¨åœ¨æ‰§è¡Œç‰¹å®šä»»åŠ¡çš„ä»£ç å—ã€‚å‡½æ•°ç”±å‡½æ•°å…³é”®å­—ï¼Œåç§°ï¼Œæ‹¬å·ï¼ˆï¼‰å£°æ˜ã€‚æ‹¬å·å¯ä»¥å¸¦å‚æ•°ã€‚å¦‚æœä¸€ä¸ªå‡½æ•°å¸¦æœ‰ä¸€ä¸ªå‚æ•°ï¼Œå®ƒå°†è¢«å¸¦å‚æ•°è°ƒç”¨ã€‚å‡½æ•°ä¹Ÿå¯ä»¥é‡‡ç”¨é»˜è®¤å‚æ•°ã€‚å¯ä»¥é€šè¿‡ä¸¤ç§æ–¹å¼å£°æ˜æˆ–åˆ›å»ºå‡½æ•°ï¼š

*   _å£°æ˜åŠŸèƒ½_
*   _è¡¨è¾¾åŠŸèƒ½_
*   _åŒ¿ååŠŸèƒ½_
*   _ç®­å¤´åŠŸèƒ½_

### `Function Declaration`

```js
//function without parameter

function functionName(){
// code goes here
}
functionName() // calling function by its name and with parentheses

//function without parameter

function addTwoNumbers() {
  var numOne = 10;
  var numTwo = 20;
  var sum = numOne + numTwo;
  console.log(sum);
}
addTwoNumbers(); // function has to be called to be executed by it name

// function with one parameter

function functionName(parm1){
  //code goes her
}
functionName(parm1); // during calling or invoking one argument needed

function areaOfCircle(r){
  let area = Math.PI * r * r;
  return area;
}
console.log(areaOfCircle(10)) // should be called with one argument

function square(number) {
  return number * number;
}
console.log(square(10));

// function with two parameters
function functionName(parm1, parm2){
  //code goes her
}
functionName(parm1,parm2); // during calling or invoking two arguments needed

// Function without parameter doesn't take input, so lets make a parameter with parameter
function sumTwoNumbers(numOne, numTwo) {
  var sum = numOne + numTwo;
  console.log(sum);
}
sumTwoNumbers(10, 20); // calling functions

// If a function doesn't return it doesn't store data, so it should return
function sumTwoNumbersAndReturn(numOne, numTwo) {
  var sum = numOne + numTwo;
  return sum;
}
console.log(sumTwoNumbersAndReturn(10, 20));

function printFullName(firstName, lastName) {
  return `${firstName} ${lastName}`;
}
console.log(printFullName('Asabeneh', 'Yetayeh'));
console.log(printFullName('Dean', 'Phan'));

// function with multiple parameters
function functionName(parm1, parm2, parm3,...){
  //code goes ther
}
functionName(parm1,parm2,parm3,...) // during calling or invoking three arguments needed


// this function takes array as a parameter and sum up the numbers in the array
function sumArrayValues(arr) {
  var sum = 0;
  for (var i = 0; i < arr.length; i++) {
    sum = sum + numbers[i];
  }
  return sum;
}
const numbers = [1, 2, 3, 4, 5];
console.log(sumArrayValues(numbers));
  

const areaOfCircle = (radius) => {
      let area = Math.PI * radius * radius;
      return area;
    }
console.log(areaOfCircle(10))
```

### `Function Expression`

```js
//Declaration function
function square(n) {
  return n * n;
}
console.log(square(2)); // -> 4
// Function expression
const square = function(n) {
  return n * n;
};
console.log(square(2)); // -> 4
```

### `Anonymous Function`

```js
// Self invoking functions
(function(n) {
  return n * n;
})(2);

const x = (function(n) {
  return n * n;
})(2);
console.log(x) // 4
```

### `Arrow Function`

```js
const square = n => {
  return n * n;
};
console.log(square(2)); // -> 4

// if we have only one line, it can be written as follows
// Explicit return
const square = n => n * n; // -> 4
```

### `Arrow Function vs Declaration Function`

ç®­å¤´åŠŸèƒ½å’Œå¸¸è§„åŠŸèƒ½ä¸å®Œå…¨ç›¸åŒã€‚

`Object`
--------

ä¸€åˆ‡éƒ½å¯ä»¥æ˜¯å¯¹è±¡ï¼Œå¯¹è±¡ç¡®å®å…·æœ‰å±æ€§ï¼Œå±æ€§å…·æœ‰å€¼ã€‚åˆ›å»ºå¯¹è±¡æ–‡å­—ã€‚è¦åˆ›å»ºå¯¹è±¡æ–‡å­—ï¼Œæˆ‘ä»¬ä½¿ç”¨ä¸¤ä¸ªå¤§æ‹¬å·ã€‚ç©ºç‰©ä½“

ç°åœ¨ï¼Œäººå‘˜å¯¹è±¡å…·æœ‰firstNameï¼ŒlastNameï¼Œå¹´é¾„ï¼Œä½ç½®ï¼ŒæŠ€èƒ½å’ŒgetFullNameå±æ€§ã€‚getFullNameæ˜¯personå¯¹è±¡å†…éƒ¨çš„å‡½æ•°ï¼Œæˆ‘ä»¬ç§°ä¹‹ä¸ºæ–¹æ³•ã€‚åœ¨_è¿™ä¸ª_å…³é”®çš„è¯æ˜¯æŒ‡å¯¹è±¡çš„å¯¹è±¡itself.Exampleï¼š

```js
const person = {
  firstName: 'Asabeneh',
  lastName: 'Yetayeh',
  age: 100,
  location: 'Helsinki',
  skills: [
    'HTML',
    'CSS',
    'JavaScript',
    'React',
    'Node',
    'MongoDB',
    'Python',
    'D3.js'
  ],
  getFullName: function() {
    return `${this.firstName}${this.lastName}`;
  }
};

const rectangle = {
  length: 20,
  width: 20,
  getArea: function() {
    return this.length * this.width;
  },
  getPerimeter: function() {
    return 2 * (this.length + this.width);
  }
};
```

ä»å¯¹è±¡è·å–å€¼ï¼š

```js
  const person = {
    firstName:'Asabeneh',
    lastName:'Yetayeh',
    age:100,
    location:'Helsinki',
    skills:['HTML', 'CSS', 'JavaScript', 'React','Node','MongoDB', 'Python', 'D3.js']
    getFullName:function() {
      return `${this.firstName}${this.lastName}`
    }
  }
  console.log(person.firstName);
  console.log(person.lastName);
  console.log(person.getFullName());
  // value can be accessed
  console.log(person['age');
  console.log(person['location']);
```

åœ¨å¯¹è±¡ä¸­è®¾ç½®æ–°é”®


### `Object Methods`

_Object.assign_ï¼šå¤åˆ¶å¯¹è±¡è€Œä¸ä¿®æ”¹åŸå§‹å¯¹è±¡

```js
const person = {
  name: 'Asabeneh',
  age: 200,
  country: 'Finland',
  skills: ['HTML', 'CSS', 'JS'],
  address: {
    street: 'Heitamienkatu 16',
    pobox: 2002,
    city: 'Helsinki'
  },
  getPersonInfo: function() {
    return `I am ${this.name} and I live in ${this.country}. I am ${this.age}.`;
  }
};

//Object methods: Object.assign, Object.keys, Object.values, Object.entries
//hasOwnProperty

const copyPerson = Object.assign({}, person);
console.log(copyPerson);
```

_Object.keys_ï¼šå°†å¯¹è±¡çš„é”®ä½œä¸ºæ•°ç»„è·å–

```js
const keys = Object.keys(copyPerson);
console.log(keys); //['name', 'age', 'country', 'skills', 'address', 'getPersonInfo']
const address = Object.keys(copyPerson.address);
console.log(address); //['street', 'pobox', 'city']
```

_Object.values_ï¼šä»¥æ•°ç»„å½¢å¼è·å–å¯¹è±¡çš„å€¼

```js
const values = Object.values(copyPerson);
console.log(values);
```

_Object.entries_ï¼šè·å–æ•°ç»„ä¸­çš„é”®å’Œå€¼

```js
const entries = Object.entries(copyPerson);
console.log(entries);
```

_hasOwnProperty_ï¼šæ£€æŸ¥å¯¹è±¡ä¸­æ˜¯å¦å­˜åœ¨ç‰¹å®šçš„é”®æˆ–å±æ€§

```js
console.log(copyPerson.hasOwnProperty('name'));
console.log(copyPerson.hasOwnProperty('score'));
```

### `Date Object`

åœ¨JavaScriptä¸­ï¼Œå½“å‰æ—¶é—´å’Œæ—¥æœŸæ˜¯ä½¿ç”¨JavaScript Dateå¯¹è±¡åˆ›å»ºçš„ã€‚æå–æ—¥æœŸå¯¹è±¡å€¼çš„ä¸€äº›æ–¹æ³•ï¼š_getFullYearï¼ˆï¼‰ï¼ŒgetMonthsï¼ˆï¼‰ï¼ŒgetDateï¼ˆï¼‰ï¼ŒgetDayï¼ˆï¼‰ï¼ŒgetHoursï¼ˆï¼‰ï¼ŒgetMinutes_

```js
const now = new Date ();
const year = now.getFullYear(); // return year
const month = now.getMonth() + 1; // return month(0 - 11)
const date = now.getDate(); // return date (1 - 31)
const hours = now.getHours(); // return number (0 - 23)
const minutes = now.getMinutes();// return number (0 -59)
console.log(`${date}/${month}/${year} ${hours}:${minutes}`)
```


`JSON`
------

JSONä»£è¡¨JavaScript Object Notationã€‚JSONè¯­æ³•æ´¾ç”Ÿè‡ªJavaScriptå¯¹è±¡è¡¨ç¤ºæ³•è¯­æ³•ï¼Œä½†JSONæ ¼å¼ä»…æ˜¯æ–‡æœ¬æˆ–å­—ç¬¦ä¸²ã€‚JSONæ˜¯ç”¨äºå­˜å‚¨å’Œä¼ è¾“çš„è½»é‡æ•°æ®æ ¼å¼ã€‚JSONé€šå¸¸åœ¨æ•°æ®ä»æœåŠ¡å™¨å‘é€åˆ°å®¢æˆ·ç«¯æ—¶ä½¿ç”¨ã€‚JSONæ˜¯XMLçš„ä¸€ç§æ˜“äºä½¿ç”¨çš„æ›¿ä»£æ–¹æ³•ã€‚

### `Converting JSON to JavaScript Object`

é€šå¸¸ï¼Œæˆ‘ä»¬ä»HTTPå“åº”æˆ–æ–‡ä»¶ä¸­è·å–JSONæ•°æ®ï¼Œä½†æ˜¯æˆ‘ä»¬å¯ä»¥å°†JSONå­˜å‚¨ä¸ºå­—ç¬¦ä¸²ï¼Œå¹¶ä¸”ä¸ºäº†æ¼”ç¤ºèµ·è§ï¼Œæˆ‘ä»¬å¯ä»¥æ›´æ”¹ä¸ºObjectã€‚åœ¨JavaScriptä¸­ï¼Œå…³é”®å­—_JSON_å…·æœ‰_parseï¼ˆï¼‰_å’Œ_stringifyï¼ˆï¼‰_æ–¹æ³•ã€‚å½“æˆ‘ä»¬æƒ³å°†JSONæ›´æ”¹ä¸ºå¯¹è±¡æ—¶ï¼Œæˆ‘ä»¬ä½¿ç”¨_JSON.parseï¼ˆï¼‰_è§£æJSON ã€‚å½“æˆ‘ä»¬æƒ³å°†å¯¹è±¡æ›´æ”¹ä¸ºJSONæ—¶ï¼Œæˆ‘ä»¬ä½¿ç”¨_JSON.stringifyï¼ˆï¼‰_ã€‚

#### `JSON.parse()`

```js
JSON.parse(json[, reviver])
// json or text , the data
// reviver is an optional callback function
```

```js
const usersText = `{
"users":[
  {
    "firstName":"Asabeneh",
    "lastName":"Yetayeh",
    "age":250,
    "email":"asab@asb.com"
  },
  {
    "firstName":"Alex",
    "lastName":"James",
    "age":25,
    "email":"alex@alex.com"
  },
  {
  "firstName":"Lidiya",
  "lastName":"Tekle",
  "age":28,
  "email":"lidiya@lidiya.com"
  }
]
}`

const usersObj = JSON.parse(usersText, undefined, 4)
console.log(usersObj)
```

### `Using a reviver function with JSON.parse()`

è¦å°†reviverå‡½æ•°ç”¨ä½œæ ¼å¼åŒ–ç¨‹åºï¼Œæˆ‘ä»¬å°†è¦æ ¼å¼åŒ–çš„é”®æ”¾åœ¨åå­—å’Œå§“æ°å€¼ä¹‹é—´ã€‚è®©æˆ‘ä»¬è¯´ï¼Œæˆ‘ä»¬æœ‰å…´è¶£æ ¼å¼åŒ–JSONæ•°æ®çš„firstNameå’ŒlastNameã€‚

```js
const usersText = `{
"users":[
  {
    "firstName":"Asabeneh",
    "lastName":"Yetayeh",
    "age":250,
    "email":"asab@asb.com"
  },
  {
    "firstName":"Alex",
    "lastName":"James",
    "age":25,
    "email":"alex@alex.com"
  },
  {
  "firstName":"Lidiya",
  "lastName":"Tekle",
  "age":28,
  "email":"lidiya@lidiya.com"
  }
]
}`

const usersObj = JSON.parse(usersText, (key, value) => {
  let newValue =
    typeof value == 'string' && key != 'email' ? value.toUpperCase() : value
  return newValue
})
console.log(usersObj)
```

è¯¥_JSON.parseï¼ˆï¼‰æ¥_æ˜¯ä½¿ç”¨èµ·æ¥éå¸¸é¡ºæ‰‹ã€‚æ‚¨ä¸å¿…ä¼ é€’å¯é€‰å‚æ•°ï¼Œåªéœ€å°†å…¶ä¸å¿…éœ€å‚æ•°ä¸€èµ·ä½¿ç”¨ï¼Œæ‚¨å°†è·å¾—å¾ˆå¤šæ”¶ç›Šã€‚

### `Converting Object to JSON`

å½“æˆ‘ä»¬æƒ³å°†å¯¹è±¡æ›´æ”¹ä¸ºJSONæ—¶ï¼Œæˆ‘ä»¬ä½¿ç”¨_JSON.stringifyï¼ˆï¼‰_ã€‚stringifyæ–¹æ³•é‡‡ç”¨ä¸€ä¸ªå¿…éœ€å‚æ•°å’Œä¸¤ä¸ªå¯é€‰å‚æ•°ã€‚æ›¿æ¢å™¨ç”¨ä½œè¿‡æ»¤å™¨ï¼Œç©ºé—´ä¸ºå‡¹ç—•ã€‚å¦‚æœæˆ‘ä»¬ä¸æƒ³ä»å¯¹è±¡ä¸­è¿‡æ»¤æ‰ä»»ä½•é”®ï¼Œæˆ‘ä»¬å¯ä»¥ä¼ é€’æœªå®šä¹‰çš„é”®ã€‚

```js
// json or text , the data
```

### `Using a Filter Array with JSON.stringify`

ç°åœ¨ï¼Œè®©æˆ‘ä»¬ä½¿ç”¨æ›¿æ¢å™¨ä½œä¸ºè¿‡æ»¤å™¨ã€‚ç”¨æˆ·å¯¹è±¡çš„é”®åˆ—è¡¨å¾ˆé•¿ï¼Œä½†æ˜¯æˆ‘ä»¬åªå¯¹å…¶ä¸­çš„å‡ ä¸ªæ„Ÿå…´è¶£ã€‚æˆ‘ä»¬å°†è¦ä¿ç•™çš„é”®æ”¾åœ¨ç¤ºä¾‹ä¸­æ‰€ç¤ºçš„æ•°ç»„ä¸­ï¼Œå¹¶ç”¨å®ƒä»£æ›¿æ›¿æ¢ç¬¦ã€‚

```js

  firstName: 'Asabeneh',
  lastName: 'Yetayeh',
  country: 'Finland',
  city: 'Helsinki',
  email: 'alex@alex.com',
  skills: ['HTML', 'CSS', 'JavaScript', 'React', 'Pyhton'],
  age: 250,
  isLoggedIn: false,

```

```shell
    "lastName": "Yetayeh",
    "country": "Finland",
    "city": "Helsinki",
    "age": 250
```

### `Exercises Level 2`

1.  ä»…ä½¿ç”¨firstNameï¼ŒlastNameå’ŒæŠ€èƒ½å±æ€§å¯¹å­¦ç”Ÿå¯¹è±¡è¿›è¡Œå­—ç¬¦ä¸²åŒ–

`Higher Order Function`
-----------------------

é«˜é˜¶å‡½æ•°æ˜¯å°†å…¶ä»–å‡½æ•°ä½œä¸ºå‚æ•°æˆ–å°†å‡½æ•°ä½œä¸ºå€¼è¿”å›çš„å‡½æ•°ã€‚ä½œä¸ºå‚æ•°ä¼ é€’çš„å‡½æ•°ç§°ä¸ºå›è°ƒã€‚

### `Callback`

å›è°ƒæ˜¯ä¸€ä¸ªå¯ä»¥ä½œä¸ºå‚æ•°ä¼ é€’ç»™å…¶ä»–å‡½æ•°çš„å‡½æ•°ã€‚è¯·å‚è§ä¸‹é¢çš„ç¤ºä¾‹ã€‚

```js
// a callback function, the function could be any name
const callback = (n) => {
  return n ** 2
}
â€‹
// function take other function as a callback
function cube(callback, n) {
  return callback(n) * n
}
â€‹
console.log(cube(callback, 3))
```

### `Returning function`

é«˜é˜¶å‡½æ•°å°†å‡½æ•°è¿”å›ä¸ºå€¼

```js
// Higher order function returning an other function
const higherOrder = n => {
  const doSomething = m => {
    const doWhatEver = t => {
      return 2 * n + 3 * m + t
    }
    return doWhatEver
  }
â€‹
  return doSomething
}
console.log(higherOrder(2)(3)(10))
```

è®©æˆ‘ä»¬çœ‹çœ‹æˆ‘ä»¬æ˜¯å¦ä½¿ç”¨äº†å›è°ƒå‡½æ•°ï¼Œä¾‹å¦‚_forEach_æ–¹æ³•ä½¿ç”¨äº†å›è°ƒå‡½æ•°ã€‚

```js
const numbers = [1, 2, 3, 4]
â€‹
const sumArray = arr => {
  let sum = 0
  const callBack = function(element) {
    sum += element
  }
  numbers.forEach(callback)
  return sum

}
console.log(sumArray(numbers))
```

ä¸Šé¢çš„ç¤ºä¾‹å¯ä»¥ç®€åŒ–å¦‚ä¸‹ï¼š

```js
const numbers = [1, 2, 3, 4]
â€‹
const sumArray = arr => {
  let sum = 0
  numbers.forEach(function(element) {
    sum += element
  })
  return sum

}
console.log(sumArray(numbers))
```

### `setting time`

åœ¨JavaScriptä¸­ï¼Œæˆ‘ä»¬å¯ä»¥åœ¨ä¸€å®šçš„æ—¶é—´é—´éš”å†…æ‰§è¡ŒæŸäº›æ´»åŠ¨ï¼Œä¹Ÿå¯ä»¥å®‰æ’ï¼ˆç­‰å¾…ï¼‰ä¸€æ®µæ—¶é—´ä»¥æ‰§è¡ŒæŸäº›æ´»åŠ¨ã€‚

*   setInterval
*   setTimeout

#### `setInterval`

åœ¨JavaScriptä¸­ï¼Œæˆ‘ä»¬ä½¿ç”¨setIntervalé«˜é˜¶å‡½æ•°åœ¨ä¸€å®šæ—¶é—´é—´éš”å†…è¿ç»­è¿›è¡ŒæŸäº›æ´»åŠ¨ã€‚setIntervalå…¨å±€æ–¹æ³•ä»¥å›è°ƒå‡½æ•°å’ŒæŒç»­æ—¶é—´ä¸ºå‚æ•°ã€‚æŒç»­æ—¶é—´ä»¥æ¯«ç§’ä¸ºå•ä½ï¼Œå¹¶ä¸”å›è°ƒå°†å§‹ç»ˆåœ¨è¯¥æ—¶é—´é—´éš”å†…è°ƒç”¨ã€‚

```js
// syntax
function callBack() {
  // code goes here
}
setInterval(callback, duration)
```

```js
function sayHello() {
  console.log('Hello')
}
setInterval(sayHello, 2000) // it prints hello in every 2 seconds
```

#### `setTimeout`

åœ¨JavaScriptä¸­ï¼Œæˆ‘ä»¬ä½¿ç”¨setTimeouté«˜é˜¶å‡½æ•°åœ¨å°†æ¥çš„æŸä¸ªæ—¶é—´æ‰§è¡ŒæŸäº›æ“ä½œã€‚setTimeoutå…¨å±€æ–¹æ³•é‡‡ç”¨å›è°ƒå‡½æ•°å’ŒæŒç»­æ—¶é—´ä½œä¸ºå‚æ•°ã€‚æŒç»­æ—¶é—´ä»¥æ¯«ç§’ä¸ºå•ä½ï¼Œå¹¶ä¸”å›è°ƒç­‰å¾…è¯¥æ—¶é—´é‡ã€‚

```js
// syntax
function callback() {
  // code goes here
}
setTimeout(callback, duration) // duration in milliseconds
```

```js
function sayHello() {
  console.log('Hello')
}
setTimeout(sayHello, 2000) // it prints hello after it waits for 2 seconds.
```

### `Exercises Level 3`

1.  å°†_txt_ JSONè§£æä¸ºå¯¹è±¡ã€‚
2.  ä»_txtä¸­_å­˜å‚¨çš„å˜é‡ä¸­æ‰¾åˆ°å…·æœ‰å¾ˆå¤šæŠ€èƒ½çš„ç”¨æˆ·ã€‚

`Functional Programming`
------------------------

*   _forEach_ï¼šè¿­ä»£æ•°ç»„å…ƒç´ å¹¶ç”¨äºæ•°ç»„ã€‚å®ƒä½¿ç”¨å¸¦æœ‰å…ƒç´ å’Œç´¢å¼•å‚æ•°çš„å›è°ƒå‡½æ•°ã€‚

```js
arr.forEach(function(element, index){
  console.log(index, element)
})
// The above code can be written using arrow function
arr.forEach((element, index) => {
  console.log(index, element)
})
// The above code can be written using arrow function and explicit return
arr.forEach((element, index) => console.log(index, element));
```

*   _map_ï¼šè¿­ä»£æ•°ç»„å…ƒç´ å¹¶ä¿®æ”¹æ•°ç»„å…ƒç´ ã€‚å®ƒä½¿ç”¨å¸¦æœ‰å…ƒç´ å’Œç´¢å¼•å‚æ•°çš„å›è°ƒå‡½æ•°ï¼Œå¹¶è¿”å›ä¿®æ”¹åçš„æ•°ç»„ã€‚

```js
const modifiedArray = arr.map(function(element,index){
  return element
});
/*Arrow function and explicit return
const modifiedArray = arr.map((element,index) => element);
*/
//Example
const numbers = [1,2,3,4,5];
const numbersSquare = numbers.map((num) => num * num) 
console.log(numbersSquare) // [1,4,9,16,25]
const names = ['Asabeneh', 'Mathias', 'Elias', 'Brook'];
const namesToUpperCase = names.map((name) => name.toUpperCase());
console.log(namesToUpperCase) //['ASABENEH', 'MATHIAS', 'ELIAS', 'BROOK']
const countries = [
  'Albania',
  'Bolivia',
  'Canada',
  'Denmark',
  'Ethiopia',
  'Finland',
  'Germany',
  'Hungary',
  'Ireland',
  'Japan',
  'Kenya'
];
const countriesToUpperCase = countries.map(function(country){
  return country.toUpperCase();
});
console.log(countriesToUpperCase)
// ['ALBANIA', 'BOLIVIA', 'CANADA', 'DENMARK', 'ETHIOPIA', 'FINLAND', 'GERMANY', 'HUNGARY', 'IRELAND', 'JAPAN', 'KENYA']
/*
// Arrow function
const countriesToUpperCase = countries.map((country) => {
  return country.toUpperCase();
})
//Explicit return arrow function
const countriesToUpperCase = countries.map(country => country.toUpperCase());
*/
```

*   _è¿‡æ»¤å™¨_ï¼šè¿‡æ»¤å‡ºæ»¡è¶³è¿‡æ»¤æ¡ä»¶çš„é¡¹ç›®

```js
// Filter countries containing land
const countriesContainingLand = countries.filter(country => country.includes('land'));
console.log(countriesContainingLand )  //['Finland', 'Ireland']

const countriesEndByia = countries.filter(country => country.includes('ia'));
console.log(countriesEndByia) //['Albania', 'Bolivia','Ethiopia']

const countriesHaveFiveLetters = countries.filter(country => country.length === 5);
console.log(countriesHaveFiveLetters ) //  ['Japan', 'Kenya']

const scores = [{name:'Asabeneh', score:95},{name:'Mathias', score:80},{name:'Elias', score:50},{name:'Martha', score:85},{name:'John', score:100}];

const scoresGreaterEight = scores.filter((score) => score.score > 80);
console.log(scoresGreaterEight) //[{name: 'Asabeneh', score: 95}, {name: 'Martha', score: 85},{name: 'John', score: 100}]
```

*   _reduce_ï¼š_reduce_å¸¦æœ‰å›è°ƒå‡½æ•°ã€‚å›è°ƒå‡½æ•°å°†ç´¯åŠ å™¨å’Œå½“å‰å€¼ä½œä¸ºå‚æ•°ï¼Œå¹¶è¿”å›ä¸€ä¸ªå€¼ï¼š

```js
  const numbers = [1,2,3,4,5];
  const sum = numbers.reduce((accum, curr)=> accum + curr);

  console.log(sum); // 15
```

*   _every_ï¼šæ£€æŸ¥æ‰€æœ‰å…ƒç´ åœ¨ä¸€æ–¹é¢æ˜¯å¦ç›¸ä¼¼ã€‚å®ƒè¿”å›å¸ƒå°”å€¼

```js
const names = ['Asabeneh', 'Mathias', 'Elias', 'Brook'];
const bools = [true, true, true, true];
const result = bools.every((b)=> {
  return b === true;
});

console.log(result) //true

const checkType = names.every((name) => typeof name ==='string');

console.log(checkDataTypes) // true;
```

*   _ä¸€äº›_ï¼šæ£€æŸ¥æŸäº›å…ƒç´ åœ¨ä¸€æ–¹é¢æ˜¯å¦ç›¸ä¼¼ã€‚å®ƒè¿”å›å¸ƒå°”å€¼

```js
const names = ['Asabeneh', 'Mathias', 'Elias', 'Brook'];
const bools = [true, true, true, true];
const result = bools.some((b)=> {
  return b === true;
});
console.log(result) //true
const checkType = names.some((name) => typeof name ==='number');
console.log(checkDataTypes) // false
```

*   _find_ï¼šè¿”å›æ»¡è¶³æ¡ä»¶çš„ç¬¬ä¸€ä¸ªå…ƒç´ 

```js
const names = ['Asabeneh', 'Mathias', 'Elias', 'Brook'];
const ages = [24, 22,25,32,35,18];
const result = names.find(name =>  name.length > 7);
console.log(result) // Asabeneh
const age = ages.find((age) => age < 20);
console.log(age) // 18
```

*   _findIndex_ï¼šè¿”å›æ»¡è¶³æ¡ä»¶çš„ç¬¬ä¸€ä¸ªå…ƒç´ çš„ä½ç½®

```js
const names = ['Asabeneh', 'Mathias', 'Elias', 'Brook'];
const ages = [24, 22,25,32,35,18];
const result = names.findIndex(name =>  name.length > 7);
console.log(result) // 0

const age = ages.findIndex((age) => age < 20);
console.log(age) // 5
```

*   _sort_ï¼šsortæ–¹æ³•å°†æ•°ç»„å…ƒç´ æŒ‰å‡åºæˆ–é™åºæ’åˆ—ã€‚é»˜è®¤æƒ…å†µä¸‹ï¼Œ_**sortï¼ˆï¼‰**_æ–¹æ³•å°†å€¼ä½œä¸ºå­—ç¬¦ä¸²_**æ’åº**_ï¼Œè¿™å¯¹äºå­—ç¬¦ä¸²æ•°ç»„é¡¹æœ‰æ•ˆï¼Œä½†ä¸é€‚ç”¨äºæ•°å­—ã€‚å¦‚æœæ•°å­—å€¼æŒ‰å­—ç¬¦ä¸²æ’åºï¼Œåˆ™ä¼šç»™æˆ‘ä»¬é”™è¯¯çš„ç»“æœã€‚æ’åºæ–¹æ³•ä¿®æ”¹åŸå§‹æ•°ç»„ã€‚å»ºè®®æ‚¨åœ¨å¼€å§‹åˆ†ç±»ä¹‹å‰å¤åˆ¶åŸå§‹æ–‡æ¡£ã€‚
    
*   _å­—ç¬¦ä¸²å€¼æ’åº_
    

```js
const products = ['Milk', 'Coffee', 'Sugar', 'Honey', 'Apple', 'Carrot'];
console.log(products.sort()) // ['Apple', 'Carrot', 'Coffee', 'Honey', 'Milk', 'Sugar']
//Now the original products array  is also sorted
```

*   _æ•°å€¼æ’åº_

å¦‚æ‚¨åœ¨ä¸‹é¢çš„ç¤ºä¾‹ä¸­çœ‹åˆ°çš„ï¼ŒæŒ‰å‡åºæ’åºåï¼Œç¬¬100ä½æ’åœ¨ç¬¬ä¸€ä½ã€‚Sortå°†é¡¹ç›®è½¬æ¢ä¸ºstringï¼Œå› ä¸ºæ¯”è¾ƒäº†'100'å’Œå…¶ä»–æ•°å­—ï¼Œå³å­—ç¬¦ä¸²'100'çš„å¼€å¤´å˜ä¸ºæœ€å°çš„æ•°å­—1ã€‚ä¸ºé¿å…è¿™ç§æƒ…å†µï¼Œæˆ‘ä»¬åœ¨sortæ–¹æ³•å†…éƒ¨ä½¿ç”¨äº†ä¸€ä¸ªæ¯”è¾ƒå›è°ƒå‡½æ•°ï¼Œè¯¥å‡½æ•°è¿”å›ä¸€ä¸ªè´Ÿæ•°ï¼Œé›¶æˆ–æ­£æ•°ã€‚

```js
const numbers = [9.81, 3.14, 100, 37]
// Using sort method to sort number items provide a wrong result. see below
console.log(numbers.sort()) //[100, 3.14, 37, 9.81]
numbers.sort(function(a, b) {
return a - b;
})

console.log(numbers) // [3.14, 9.81, 37, 100]
numbers.sort(function(a, b) {
return b - a;
});
console.log(numbers) //[100, 37, 9.81, 3.14]
```

*   _æ’åºå¯¹è±¡æ•°ç»„_

æ¯å½“æˆ‘ä»¬å¯¹æ•°ç»„ä¸­çš„å¯¹è±¡è¿›è¡Œæ’åºæ—¶ã€‚æˆ‘ä»¬ä½¿ç”¨å¯¹è±¡é”®è¿›è¡Œæ¯”è¾ƒã€‚è®©æˆ‘ä»¬çœ‹ä¸‹é¢çš„ä¾‹å­ã€‚

```js
objArr.sort(function(a, b) {
  if (a.key < b.key) return -1;
  if (a.key > b.key) return 1;
  return 0;
});

// or

objArr.sort(function(a, b) {
  if (a['key'] < b['key']) return -1;
  if (a['key'] > b['key']) return 1;
  return 0;
});

const users = [{name:'Asabeneh', age:150}, {name:'Brook', age:50}, {name:'Eyo', age:100},{name:'Elias', age:22}];
users.sort((a, b) => {
  if (a.age < b.age) return -1;
  if (a.age > b.age) return 1;
  return 0;
});

console.log(users); // sorted ascending
//[{â€¦}, {â€¦}, {â€¦}, {â€¦}]
```

`Destructuring and Spread`
--------------------------

è§£æ„æ˜¯ä¸€ç§è§£å‹ç¼©æ•°ç»„å’Œå¯¹è±¡å¹¶åˆ†é…ç»™ä¸åŒå˜é‡çš„æ–¹æ³•ã€‚

### `Destructing Arrays`

```js
  const numbers = [1, 2,3];
  let [numOne, numTwo, numThree] = numbers;
  console.log(numOne, numTwo, numThree) // 1,2,3
  const names = ['Asabeneh', 'Brook', 'David', 'John']
  let [firstPerson, secondPerson, ThirdPerson, fourth Person] = names;
  console.log(firstName, secondPerson,thirdPerson, fourthPerson) //Asabeneh, Brook, David, John
  const scientificConstants = [2.72, 3.14, 9.81, 37, 100];
  let [e, pi, gravity, bodyTemp, boilingTemp] = scientificConstants
  console.log(e,pi,gravity, bodyTemp, boilingTemp) //2.72, 3.14, 9.81, 37, 100
```

å¦‚æœæˆ‘ä»¬æƒ³è·³è¿‡æ•°ç»„ä¸­çš„å€¼ï¼Œè¯·ä½¿ç”¨å…¶ä»–é€—å·ã€‚é€—å·æœ‰åŠ©äºçœç•¥è¯¥ç´¢å¼•å¤„çš„å€¼

```js
  const numbers = [1, 2,3];
  let [numOne, , , numThree] = numbers; //2 is omitted
  console.log(numOne,, numThree) // 1,2,3
  const names = ['Asabeneh', 'Brook', 'David', 'John']
  let [, secondPerson, , fourth Person] = name; // first and third person is omitted
  console.log(secondPerson, fourthPerson) //Brook, John
```

å¦‚æœè¯¥ç´¢å¼•çš„æ•°ç»„å€¼æœªå®šä¹‰ï¼Œæˆ‘ä»¬å¯ä»¥ä½¿ç”¨é»˜è®¤å€¼ï¼š

```js
const names = [undefined, 'Brook', 'David'];
let [firstPerson = 'Asabeneh', secondPerson, thirdPerson, fourthPerson = 'John' ] = names;
console.log(firstPerson, secondPerson, thirdPerson, fourthPerson) // Asabeneh Brook David John
```

#### `Destructuring Object`

å½“æˆ‘ä»¬è§£æ„å˜é‡æ—¶ï¼Œç”¨äºè§£æ„çš„å˜é‡ååº”è¯¥ä¸å¯¹è±¡çš„é”®æˆ–å±æ€§å®Œå…¨ç›¸åŒã€‚è¯·å‚è§ä¸‹é¢çš„ç¤ºä¾‹ã€‚

```js
const rectangle = {
  width: 20,
  height:10,
  area: 200
}
let {width, height, area, perimeter} = rectangle;
console.log(width, height, area, perimeter) //20 10 200 undefined
```

#### `Renaming during structuring`

```js
const rectangle = {
  width: 20,
  height:10,
  area: 200
}
let {width:w, heigh:h, area:a, perimeter:p} = rectangle;
console.log(w, h, a, p) //20 10 200 undefined
```

å¦‚æœåœ¨å¯¹è±¡ä¸­æ‰¾ä¸åˆ°å…³é”®å­—ï¼Œåˆ™å˜é‡å°†åˆ†é…ä¸ºundefinedã€‚å¦‚æœå¯†é’¥ä¸åœ¨å¯¹è±¡ä¸­ï¼Œæˆ‘ä»¬å¯ä»¥åœ¨å£°æ˜è¿‡ç¨‹ä¸­æä¾›é»˜è®¤å€¼ã€‚å‚è§ç¤ºä¾‹ã€‚

```js
const rectangle = {
  width: 20,
  height:10,
  area: 200
}
let {width, heigh, area, perimeter = 60} = rectangle;
console.log(width, height, area, perimeter)  //20 10 200 60

//Lets modify the object:width to 30 and perimeter to 80
const rectangle = {
  width: 30,
  height:10,
  area: 200,
  perimeter:80
}
let {width, heigh, area, perimeter = 60} = rectangle;
console.log(width, height, area, perimeter) //20 10 200 80
```

è§£æ„é”®ä½œä¸ºåŠŸèƒ½å‚æ•°ã€‚è®©æˆ‘ä»¬åˆ›å»ºä¸€ä¸ªæ¥å—çŸ©å½¢å¯¹è±¡çš„å‡½æ•°ï¼Œå®ƒè¿”å›çŸ©å½¢çš„å‘¨é•¿ã€‚

```js
    // Without destructuring
    const rect = {
      width:20,
      height:10
    }
    const calculatePerimeter = (rectangle) => {
      return 2 * (rectangle.width + rectangle.height)
    }
    console.log(calculatePerimeter(rect)) // 60
    //with destructuring

     const calculatePerimeter = ({width, height}) => {
      return 2 * (width + height)
    }

    console.log(calculatePerimeter(rect)) // 60

    //Another Example
const person = {
  firstName: 'Asabeneh',
  lastName: 'Yetayeh',
  age: 200,
  country: 'Finland',
  job: 'Instructor and Developer',
  skills: [
    'HTML',
    'CSS',
    'JavaScript',
    'React',
    'Redux',
    'Node',
    'MongoDB',
    'Python',
    'D3.js'
  ],
  languages: ['Amharic', 'English', 'Suomi(Finnish)']
};
// Lets create a function which give information about the person object without destructuring

const getPersonInfo = obj => {
  const skills = obj.skills;
  const formattedSkills = skills.slice(0, -1).join(', ');
  const languages = obj.languages;
  const formattedLanguages = languages.slice(0, -1).join(', ');

  return `${obj.firstName} ${obj.lastName} lives in ${obj.country}. He is  ${
    obj.age
  } years old. He is an ${obj.job}. He teaches ${formattedSkills} and ${
    skills[skills.length - 1]
  }. He speaks ${formattedLanguages} and a little bit of ${languages[2]}.`;
};
console.log(getPersonInfo(person));
// Lets create a function which give information about the person object with destructuring

const getPersonInfo = ({
  firstName,
  lastName,
  age,
  country,
  job,
  skills,
  languages
}) => {
  const formattedSkills = skills.slice(0, -1).join(', ');
  const formattedLanguages = languages.slice(0, -1).join(', ');

  return `${firstName} ${lastName} lives in ${country}. He is ${age} years old. He is an ${job}. He teaches ${formattedSkills} and ${skills[skills.length - 1]}. He speaks ${formattedLanguages} and a little bit of ${languages[2]}.`;
};
console.log(getPersonInfo(person))
/*
Asabeneh Yetayeh lives in Finland. He is  200 years old. He is an Instructor and Developer. He teaches HTML, CSS, JavaScript, React, Redux, Node, MongoDB, Python and D3.js. He speaks Amharic, English and a little bit of Suomi(Finnish)
*/
```

### `Spread or Rest Operator`

#### `Exercise: Destructuring`

```js
const constants = [2.72, 3.14, 9.81,37, 100]
const countries = ['Finland', 'Estonia', 'Sweden', 'Denmark', 'Norway']

const rectangle = {
  width:20,
  height:10,
  area:200,
  perimeter:60
}
```

1.  å°†å¸¸é‡æ•°ç»„çš„å…ƒç´ åˆ†é…ç»™eï¼Œpiï¼Œgravityï¼ŒhumanBodyTempï¼ŒwaterBoilingTempã€‚
2.  å°†countrysæ•°ç»„çš„å…ƒç´ åˆ†é…ç»™finï¼Œestï¼Œswï¼Œdenå’Œnor
3.  é€šè¿‡çŸ©å½¢å¯¹è±¡çš„å±æ€§æˆ–é”®å¯¹å…¶è¿›è¡Œè§£æ„ã€‚

`Map and Set`
-------------

`Set`
-----

é›†åˆæ˜¯å”¯ä¸€å…ƒç´ çš„é›†åˆã€‚è®©æˆ‘ä»¬çœ‹çœ‹å¦‚ä½•åˆ›å»ºä¸€ä¸ªé›†åˆ

### `Creating a set`

```js
  const companies = new Set()
```

### `Adding an element to a set`

```js
  console.log(companies.size) // 0
  companies.add('Google') // add element to the set
  companies.add('Facebook')
  companies.add('Amazon')
  companies.add('Oracle')
  companies.add('Microsoft')
  console.log(companies.size) // 5 elements in the set
```

### `Deleting an element a set`

```js
console.log(companies.delete('Google'))
console.log(companies.size) // 4 elements left in the set
```

### `Checking an element in the set`

```js
console.log(companies.has('Google')) // false
console.log(companies.has('Facebook')) // true
```

### `Clearing the set`

åˆ é™¤æ‰€æœ‰å…ƒç´ 

è¯·å‚é˜…ä¸‹é¢çš„ç¤ºä¾‹ä»¥äº†è§£å¦‚ä½•ä½¿ç”¨setã€‚

```js
const languages = [
  'English',
  'Finnish',
  'English',
  'French',
  'Spanish',
  'English',
  'French'
]
const langSet = new Set(languages)
console.log(langSet)
console.log(langSet.size)

const counts = []
const count = {}

for (const l of langSet) {
  const filteredLang = languages.filter(lng => lng === l)
  console.log(filteredLang)
  counts.push({ lang: l, count: filteredLang.length })
}
console.log(counts)
```

`Set`
-----

é›†åˆæ˜¯å…ƒç´ çš„é›†åˆã€‚é›†åªèƒ½åŒ…å«å”¯ä¸€å…ƒç´ ã€‚è®©æˆ‘ä»¬çœ‹çœ‹å¦‚ä½•åˆ›å»ºä¸€ä¸ªé›†åˆ

### `Creating an empty set`

```js
const companies = new Set()
console.log(companies)
```

### `Creating set from array`

```js
const languages = [
  'English',
  'Finnish',
  'English',
  'French',
  'Spanish',
  'English',
  'French'
]

const setOfLangauges = new Set(languages)
console.log(setOfLangauges)
```

```shell
Set(4) {"English", "Finnish", "French", "Spanish"}
```

Setæ˜¯ä¸€ä¸ªå¯è¿­ä»£çš„å¯¹è±¡ï¼Œæˆ‘ä»¬å¯ä»¥è¿­ä»£æ¯ä¸ªå…ƒç´ ã€‚

```js
const languages = [
  'English',
  'Finnish',
  'English',
  'French',
  'Spanish',
  'English',
  'French'
]

const setOfLangauges = new Set(languages)

for (const language of setOfLangauges) {
  console.log(language)
}
```

```shell
  English
  Finnish
  French
  Spanish
```

### `Adding an element to a set`

```js
const companies = new Set() // creating an empty set
console.log(companies.size) // 0

companies.add('Google') // add element to the set
companies.add('Facebook')
companies.add('Amazon')
companies.add('Oracle')
companies.add('Microsoft')

console.log(companies.size) // 5 elements in the set
console.log(companies)
```

```shell
Set(5) {"Google", "Facebook", "Amazon", "Oracle", "Microsoft"}
```

æˆ‘ä»¬è¿˜å¯ä»¥ä½¿ç”¨å¾ªç¯å°†å…ƒç´ æ·»åŠ åˆ°é›†åˆä¸­ã€‚

```js
const companies = ['Google', 'Facebook', 'Amazon', 'Oracle', 'Microsoft']
setOfCompanies = new Set()
for (const company of companies) {
  setOfCompanies.add(company)
}
```

```shell
Set(5) {"Google", "Facebook", "Amazon", "Oracle", "Microsoft"}

```

### `Deleting an element a set`

æˆ‘ä»¬å¯ä»¥ä½¿ç”¨deleteæ–¹æ³•ä»é›†åˆä¸­åˆ é™¤å…ƒç´ ã€‚

```js
console.log(companies.delete('Google'))
console.log(companies.size) // 4 elements left in the set
```

### `Checking an element in the set`

hasæ–¹æ³•å¯ä»¥å¸®åŠ©æ‚¨äº†è§£é›†åˆä¸­æ˜¯å¦å­˜åœ¨æŸä¸ªå…ƒç´ ã€‚

```js
console.log(companies.has('Apple')) // false
console.log(companies.has('Facebook')) // true
```

### `Clearing the set`

å®ƒä»é›†åˆä¸­åˆ é™¤æ‰€æœ‰å…ƒç´ ã€‚

```js
companies.clear()

console.log(companies)
```

è¯·å‚é˜…ä¸‹é¢çš„ç¤ºä¾‹ä»¥äº†è§£å¦‚ä½•ä½¿ç”¨setã€‚

```js
const languages = [
  'English',
  'Finnish',
  'English',
  'French',
  'Spanish',
  'English',
  'French'
]
const langSet = new Set(languages)
console.log(langSet) // Set(4) {"English", "Finnish", "French", "Spanish"}
console.log(langSet.size) // 4

const counts = []
const count = {}

for (const l of langSet) {
  const filteredLang = languages.filter(lng => lng === l)
  console.log(filteredLang) // ["English", "English", "English"]
  counts.push({ lang: l, count: filteredLang.length })
}
console.log(counts)
```

```js
[
  { lang: 'English', count: 3 },
  { lang: 'Finnish', count: 1 },
  { lang: 'French', count: 2 },
  { lang: 'Spanish', count: 1 }
]
```

å…¶ä»–ç”¨ä¾‹é›†ã€‚ä¾‹å¦‚ï¼Œè®¡ç®—æ•°ç»„ä¸­çš„å”¯ä¸€é¡¹ã€‚

```js
const numbers = [5, 3, 2, 5, 5, 9, 4, 5]
const setOfNumbers = new Set(numbers)

console.log(setOfNumbers)
```

### `Union of sets`

ä½¿ç”¨æ•£å¸ƒè¿ç®—ç¬¦å¯ä»¥æ‰¾åˆ°ä¸¤ä¸ªé›†åˆçš„å¹¶é›†ã€‚è®©æˆ‘ä»¬æ‰¾åˆ°é›†åˆAå’Œé›†åˆBçš„å¹¶é›†ï¼ˆAUBï¼‰

```js
let a = [1, 2, 3, 4, 5]
let b = [3, 4, 5, 6]
let c = [...a, ...b]

let A = new Set(a)
let B = new Set(b)
let C = new Set(c)

console.log(C)
```

### `Intersection of sets`

æŸ¥æ‰¾ä¸¤ä¸ªé›†åˆçš„äº¤é›†å¯ä»¥ä½¿ç”¨è¿‡æ»¤å™¨æ¥å®ç°ã€‚è®©æˆ‘ä»¬æ‰¾åˆ°é›†åˆAå’Œé›†åˆBçš„å¹¶é›†ï¼ˆAâˆ©Bï¼‰

```js
let a = [1, 2, 3, 4, 5]
let b = [3, 4, 5, 6]

let A = new Set(a)
let B = new Set(b)

let c = a.filter(num => B.has(num))
let C = new Set(c)

console.log(C)
```

### `Difference of sets`

ä¸ºäº†æ‰¾åˆ°ä¸¤ç»„ä¹‹é—´çš„å·®å¼‚ï¼Œå¯ä»¥ä½¿ç”¨æ»¤æ³¢å™¨æ¥å®ç°ã€‚è®©æˆ‘ä»¬æ‰¾å‡ºé›†åˆAå’Œé›†åˆBï¼ˆA \\ Bï¼‰çš„ä¸åŒä¹‹å¤„

```js
let a = [1, 2, 3, 4, 5]
let b = [3, 4, 5, 6]

let A = new Set(a)
let B = new Set(b)

let c = a.filter(num => !B.has(num))
let C = new Set(c)

console.log(C)
```

`Map`
-----

### `Creating an empty Map`

```js
const map = new Map()
console.log(map)
```

### `Creating an Map from array`

```js
countries = [
  ['Finland', 'Helsinki'],
  ['Sweden', 'Stockholm'],
  ['Norway', 'Oslo']
]
const map = new Map(countries)
console.log(map)
console.log(map.size)
```

```shell
Map(3) {"Finland" => "Helsinki", "Sweden" => "Stockholm", "Norway" => "Oslo"}
3
```

### `Adding values to the Map`

```js
const countriesMap = new Map()
console.log(countriesMap.size) // 0
countriesMap.set('Finland', 'Helsinki')
countriesMap.set('Sweden', 'Stockholm')
countriesMap.set('Norway', 'Oslo')
console.log(countriesMap)
console.log(countriesMap.size)
```

```shell
Map(3) {"Finland" => "Helsinki", "Sweden" => "Stockholm", "Norway" => "Oslo"}
3
```

### `Getting a value from Map`

```js
console.log(countriesMap.get('Finland'))
```

### `Checking key in Map`

ä½¿ç”¨_has_æ–¹æ³•æ£€æŸ¥æ˜ å°„ä¸­_æ˜¯å¦_å­˜åœ¨é”®ã€‚å®ƒè¿”å›_true_æˆ–_false_ã€‚

```js
console.log(countriesMap.has('Finland'))
```

ä½¿ç”¨å¾ªç¯ä»åœ°å›¾è·å–æ‰€æœ‰å€¼

```js
for (const country of countriesMap) {
  console.log(country)
}
```

```shell
(2) ["Finland", "Helsinki"]
(2) ["Sweden", "Stockholm"]
(2) ["Norway", "Oslo"]
```

```shell
for (const [country, city] of countriesMap){
console.log(country, city)
}
```

```shell
Finland Helsinki
Sweden Stockholm
Norway Oslo
```

```js
const countries = ['Finland', 'Sweden', 'Norway']
```

`Document Object Model (DOM)`
-----------------------------

HTMLæ–‡æ¡£çš„ç»“æ„ä¸ºJavaScriptå¯¹è±¡ã€‚æ¯ä¸ªHTMLå…ƒç´ éƒ½æœ‰ä¸åŒçš„å±æ€§ï¼Œå¯ä»¥å¸®åŠ©å¯¹å…¶è¿›è¡Œæ“ä½œã€‚å¯ä»¥ä½¿ç”¨JavaScriptè·å–ï¼Œåˆ›å»ºï¼Œé™„åŠ æˆ–åˆ é™¤HTMLå…ƒç´ ã€‚æ£€æŸ¥ä»¥ä¸‹ç¤ºä¾‹ã€‚ä½¿ç”¨JavaScripté€‰æ‹©HTMLå…ƒç´ ç±»ä¼¼äºé€‰æ‹©CSSã€‚è¦é€‰æ‹©HTMLå…ƒç´ ï¼Œæˆ‘ä»¬ä½¿ç”¨æ ‡ç­¾åç§°ï¼ŒIDï¼Œç±»åç§°ã€‚è¦åˆ›å»ºHTMLå…ƒç´ ï¼Œæˆ‘ä»¬ä½¿ç”¨æ ‡ç­¾åç§°ã€‚

### `Getting Element`

```html
<!DOCTYPE html>
  <html>
    <head>
      <title>Document Object Model/title>
    </head>
    <body>
     <h1 class='title' id='first-title'>First Title</h1>
     <h1 class='title' id='second-title'>Second Title</h1>
     <h1 class='title' id='third-title'>Third Title</h1>
     <h1></h1>
    </body>
  </html>
```

#### `Getting elements by tag name`

_**getElementsByTagNameï¼ˆï¼‰**_æ–¹æ³•è¿”å›ä¸€ä¸ªHTMLCollectionå¯¹è±¡ã€‚HTMLCollectionæ˜¯ä¸€ä¸ªç±»ä¼¼äºHTMLå…ƒç´ åˆ—è¡¨çš„æ•°ç»„ã€‚lengthå±æ€§æä¾›é›†åˆçš„å¤§å°ã€‚

```js
const allTitles = document.getElementsByTagName('h1');
console.log(allTitles) //HTMCollections
console.log(allTitles.length) // 4
for(let i = 0; i < allTitles.length; i++){
  console.log(allTitles[i]) // prints each elements in the HTMLCollection
}
```

#### `Getting elements by class name`

_**getElementsByClassNameï¼ˆï¼‰**_æ–¹æ³•è¿”å›ä¸€ä¸ªHTMLCollectionå¯¹è±¡ã€‚HTMLCollectionæ˜¯ä¸€ä¸ªç±»ä¼¼äºHTMLå…ƒç´ åˆ—è¡¨çš„æ•°ç»„ã€‚lengthå±æ€§æä¾›é›†åˆçš„å¤§å°ã€‚å¯ä»¥éå†æ‰€æœ‰HTMLCollectionå…ƒç´ ã€‚å‚è§ä¸‹é¢çš„ä¾‹å­

```js
const allTitles = document.getElementsByClassName('title');
console.log(allTitles) //HTMCollections
console.log(allTitles.length) // 4
for(let i = 0; i < allTitles.length; i++){
  console.log(allTitles[i]) // prints each elements in the HTMLCollection
}
```

#### `Getting an element by id`

_**getElementsByIdï¼ˆï¼‰**_ å®šä½å•ä¸ªHTMLå…ƒç´ ã€‚æˆ‘ä»¬ä¼ é€’ä¸å¸¦ï¼ƒçš„idä½œä¸ºå‚æ•°ã€‚

```js
let firstTitle = document.getElementById('first-title');
console.log(firstTitle) // <h1>First Title</h1>
```

#### `Getting elements by using querySelector using tag, class and id:`

_**querySelector**_ï¼šå¯ç”¨äºé€šè¿‡å…¶æ ‡ç­¾åç§°ï¼Œidæˆ–ç±»é€‰æ‹©HTMLå…ƒç´ ã€‚å¦‚æœä½¿ç”¨æ ‡ç­¾åç§°ï¼Œåˆ™ä»…é€‰æ‹©ç¬¬ä¸€ä¸ªå…ƒç´ ã€‚

```js
let firstTitle = document.querySelect('h1');// select the first available h2 element
let firstTitle = document.querySelector('#first-title'); // select id with first-title
let firstTitle = document.querySelector('.title'); // select the first available h2 element with class title
```

_**querySelectorAll**_ï¼šå¯ç”¨äºé€šè¿‡å…¶æ ‡è®°åç§°æˆ–ç±»é€‰æ‹©htmlå…ƒç´ ã€‚å®ƒè¿”å›ä¸€ä¸ªnodeListï¼Œå®ƒæ˜¯ä¸€ä¸ªç±»ä¼¼äºå¯¹è±¡çš„æ•°ç»„ï¼Œæ”¯æŒæ•°ç»„æ–¹æ³•ã€‚æˆ‘ä»¬å¯ä»¥ä½¿ç”¨_**forå¾ªç¯**_æˆ–_**forEach**_å¾ªç¯éå†æ¯ä¸ªnodeListå…ƒç´ ã€‚

```js
const allTitles = document.querySelectAll('h1');
console.log(allTitles.length) // 4
for(let i = 0; i < allTitles.length; i++){
  console.log(allTitles[i]);
}
allTitles.forEach(title => console.log(title))
const allTitles = document.querySelectorAll('.title'); // the same goes for selecting using class
```

### `Adding attribute`

åœ¨HTMLçš„å¼€å§‹æ ‡è®°ä¸­æ·»åŠ äº†ä¸€ä¸ªå±æ€§ï¼Œè¯¥å±æ€§æä¾›æœ‰å…³è¯¥å…ƒç´ çš„å…¶ä»–ä¿¡æ¯ã€‚å¸¸è§çš„HTMLå±æ€§ï¼šidï¼Œclassï¼Œsrcï¼Œstyleï¼Œhrefï¼Œdisabledï¼Œtitleï¼Œaltã€‚è®©æˆ‘ä»¬ä¸ºç¬¬å››ä¸ªæ ‡é¢˜æ·»åŠ idå’Œclassã€‚

#### `Adding attribute using setAttribute`

æ‰€è¿°_**çš„setAttributeï¼ˆï¼‰**_æ–¹æ³•è®¾ç½®ä»»ä½•HTMLå±æ€§ã€‚å®ƒä½¿ç”¨ä¸¤ä¸ªå‚æ•°ï¼Œå³å±æ€§çš„ç±»å‹å’Œå±æ€§çš„åç§°ã€‚è®©æˆ‘ä»¬ä¸ºç¬¬å››ä¸ªæ ‡é¢˜æ·»åŠ classå’Œidå±æ€§ã€‚

```js
const titles = document.querySelectorAll('h1');
titles[3].setAttribute('class', 'title');
titles[3].setAttribute('id', 'fourth-title');
```

#### `Adding attribute without setAttribute`

ä¸€äº›å±æ€§æ˜¯DOMå¯¹è±¡å±æ€§ï¼Œå¯ä»¥ç›´æ¥è®¾ç½®ã€‚ä¾‹å¦‚idå’Œclass

```js
//another way to setting an attribute
titles[3].className = 'title';
titles[3].id = 'fourth-title';
```

#### `Adding class using classList`

ç±»åˆ—è¡¨æ–¹æ³•æ˜¯é™„åŠ å…¶ä»–ç±»çš„å¥½æ–¹æ³•ã€‚å¦‚æœå­˜åœ¨ä¸€ä¸ªç±»ï¼Œå®ƒä¸ä¼šè¦†ç›–åŸå§‹ç±»

```js
//another way to setting an attribute: append the class, doesn't over ride
titles[3].classList.add('title', 'header-title')
```

### `Adding Text content`

```js
const titles = document.querySelectorAll('h1');
titles[3].textContent = 'Fourth Title';
```

### `Adding style`

è®©æˆ‘ä»¬ä¸ºæ ‡é¢˜æ·»åŠ ä¸€äº›æ ·å¼ã€‚å¦‚æœå…ƒç´ å…·æœ‰å¶æ•°ç´¢å¼•ï¼Œåˆ™å°†å…¶èµ‹äºˆç»¿è‰²ï¼Œå¦åˆ™èµ‹äºˆçº¢è‰²ã€‚

```js
const titles = document.querySelectorAll('h1');
titles.forEach((title,i) => {
  title.fontSize = '24px'; // all titles will have 24px font size
  if(i % 2 === 0){
    title.style.color = 'green';
  }
  else {
    title.style.color = 'red';
  }
})
```

### `Creating an Element`

```js
let title = document.createElement('h1');
let firstTitle = document.getElementById('first-title');
```

### `Creating elements`

```js
let firstTitle = document.getElementById('first-title');
let title
for(let i = 0; i < 3; i++){
  title = document.createElement('h1');
  title.className = 'title';
  title.style.fontSize = '24px';
}
```

### `Appending to a parent element`

```js
// creating multiple elements and appending to parent element
let title;
for(let i = 0; i < 3; i++){
  title = document.createElement('h1');
  title.className = 'title';
  title.style.fontSize = '24px';
  document.body.appendChild(title);
}
```

### `Event Listeners`

å¸¸è§çš„HTMLäº‹ä»¶ï¼šonclickï¼Œonchangeï¼Œonmouseoverï¼Œonmouseoutï¼Œonkeydownï¼Œonkeyupï¼Œonloadã€‚æˆ‘ä»¬å¯ä»¥å°†äº‹ä»¶ä¾¦å¬å™¨æ–¹æ³•æ·»åŠ åˆ°ä»»ä½•DOMå¯¹è±¡ã€‚ä½¿ç”¨use _**addEventListenerï¼ˆï¼‰**_æ–¹æ³•æ¥ä¾¦å¬HTMLå…ƒç´ ä¸Šçš„ä¸åŒäº‹ä»¶ç±»å‹ã€‚ä»¥ä¸‹æ˜¯ç‚¹å‡»ç±»å‹äº‹ä»¶çš„ç¤ºä¾‹ã€‚

```js
const button = document.querySelector('button');
button.addEventListener('click', e => {
  console.log(e.target);
});
```

### `Getting value from an input element`

æˆ‘ä»¬é€šå¸¸å¡«å†™è¡¨æ ¼ï¼Œå¹¶æ¥å—æ•°æ®è¡¨æ ¼ã€‚è¡¨å•å­—æ®µæ˜¯ä½¿ç”¨è¾“å…¥HTMLå…ƒç´ åˆ›å»ºçš„ã€‚

```html
<input type ='text' placeholder = 'Mass in Kilogram' />
<input type = 'text' placeholder = 'Height in meters' />
<button>Calculate BMI</button>
```

```js
const mass = document.querySelector('#mass');
const height = document.querySelector('#height');
const button = document.querySelector('button');
let bmi;
button.addEventListen('click', ()=>{
  bmi = mass.value * height.value;
});

console.log(bmi)
```

#### `Exercises:Document Object Model`

```html
  <!-- index.html -->
<!DOCTYPE html>
  <html>
    <head>
      <title>JavaScript for Everyone:DOM</title>
    </head>
    <body>
    <p>First Paragraph</p>
    <p>Second Paragraph</p>
    <p>Third Paragraph</p>
    <p></p>
    </body>
  </html>
```

1.  åˆ›å»ºä¸€ä¸ªindex.htmlæ–‡ä»¶ï¼Œå¹¶å¦‚ä¸Šæ‰€è¿°æ”¾ç½®å››ä¸ªpå…ƒç´ ï¼šä½¿ç”¨_**document.querySelectorï¼ˆtagnameï¼‰**_å’Œæ ‡ç­¾åè·å–ç¬¬ä¸€æ®µ
